--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/README.md:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | # Anirudh's Chat
 2 | 
 3 | [![Anirudh's Chat Demo](./public/demo.png)](https://screen.studio/share/r5ljIy7R)
 4 | 
 5 | <center><a href="https://screen.studio/share/r5ljIy7R">Watch the video!</a></center>
 6 | 
 7 | ## Background
 8 | 
 9 | MCP servers have come a long way, and it's been easier than ever to create and run MCP servers, but the only way to use them is through Claude Desktop or their code editor. There's no "ChatGPT for MCP" yet.
10 | 
11 | This was my attempt at creating a simple open source MCP playground, where I could test out MCP servers and see how they work. At its full potential, if MCP is the internet for agents, what does Chromium look like?
12 | 
13 | I also was heavily inspired by [t3.chat](https://t3.chat), which has some great features that I wanted to replicate, like the tree-based chat history.
14 | 
15 | ## Core Features
16 | 
17 | - Fully [Vercel AI SDK](https://sdk.vercel.ai/) compatible
18 | - Git-based chat history.
19 | - No database/auth required, just Node.js.
20 | 
21 | ## Getting Started
22 | 
23 | ### Prerequisites
24 | 
25 | - [Node.js](https://nodejs.org/en/download/) (v20 or higher)
26 | - [pnpm](https://pnpm.io/installation) (a faster alternative to npm)
27 | 
28 | ### Running the project
29 | 
30 | ```bash
31 | # Clone the repository
32 | git clone https://github.com/kamath/chat
33 | cd chat
34 | 
35 | # Install dependencies
36 | pnpm install
37 | 
38 | # Start the development server
39 | pnpm dev
40 | ```
41 | 


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/api/apiUtils.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { AvailableModel } from "@/sharedTypes";
 2 | import { anthropic } from "@ai-sdk/anthropic";
 3 | import { google } from "@ai-sdk/google";
 4 | import { openai } from "@ai-sdk/openai";
 5 | import { LanguageModelV1 } from "ai";
 6 | 
 7 | export function resolveModel(modelName: AvailableModel): LanguageModelV1 {
 8 |   const [provider, ...modelParts] = modelName.split("/");
 9 |   const model = modelParts.join("/");
10 |   switch (provider) {
11 |     case "google":
12 |       return google(model);
13 |     case "anthropic":
14 |       return anthropic(model);
15 |     case "openai":
16 |       return openai(model);
17 |     default:
18 |       throw new Error(`Unknown model provider: ${provider}`);
19 |   }
20 | }
21 |

/app/api/chat/route.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { streamText } from "ai";
 2 | import { getTools } from "@/lib/tools";
 3 | import { resolveModel } from "../apiUtils";
 4 | 
 5 | export async function POST(req: Request) {
 6 |   const { messages, pendingMessageConfig } = await req.json();
 7 | 
 8 |   console.log("Received pendingMessageConfig:", pendingMessageConfig);
 9 | 
10 |   const { tools, breakdown, closeClients } = await getTools();
11 | 
12 |   console.log("TOOLS", tools);
13 |   console.log("BREAKDOWN", breakdown);
14 | 
15 |   const result = streamText({
16 |     model: resolveModel(pendingMessageConfig.modelName),
17 |     tools,
18 |     toolCallStreaming: true,
19 |     system:
20 |       "You are a helpful assistant that can browse the web. You are given a prompt and you may need to browse the web to find the answer. You may not need to browse the web at all; you may already know the answer.",
21 |     messages,
22 |     maxSteps: 10,
23 |     abortSignal: req.signal,
24 |     onStepFinish: () => {
25 |       console.debug("STEP FINISHED");
26 |     },
27 |     onError: (error) => {
28 |       console.debug("ERROR", error);
29 |       throw error;
30 |     },
31 |     onFinish: async (message) => {
32 |       console.debug("FINISHED", message);
33 |       // Log the usage data to verify it's being captured
34 |       console.debug("USAGE DATA:", message.usage);
35 |       await closeClients();
36 |     },
37 |     experimental_telemetry: {
38 |       isEnabled: true,
39 |     },
40 |   });
41 |   return result.toDataStreamResponse();
42 | }

/app/api/tools/route.ts:

  1 | // TODO: Review this, was vibe-coded but works well enough.
  2 | // I think it's not working properly with nested fields,
  3 | // i.e. z.number().describe("A number").optional() return description
  4 | // but z.number().optional().describe("A number") does not.
  5 | 
  6 | import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
  7 | import { getTools } from "@/lib/tools";
  8 | import {
  9 |   ZodTypeAny,
 10 |   ZodObject,
 11 |   ZodString,
 12 |   ZodNumber,
 13 |   ZodBoolean,
 14 |   ZodOptional,
 15 |   ZodDefault,
 16 |   ZodSchema,
 17 | } from "zod";
 18 | import { readFile, unlink, writeFile } from "fs/promises";
 19 | import { join } from "path";
 20 | 
 21 | interface SerializedParameter {
 22 |   type: string;
 23 |   description?: string;
 24 |   optional?: boolean;
 25 | }
 26 | 
 27 | interface SerializedParameters {
 28 |   [key: string]: SerializedParameter;
 29 | }
 30 | 
 31 | interface SerializedTool {
 32 |   description?: string;
 33 |   parameters: SerializedParameters | { error: string; typeReceived?: string };
 34 | }
 35 | 
 36 | /**
 37 |  * Determines the basic type of a Zod schema node.
 38 |  * @param schema The Zod schema node.
 39 |  * @returns A string representing the type (e.g., 'string', 'number').
 40 |  */
 41 | function getParameterType(schema: ZodTypeAny): string {
 42 |   if (schema instanceof ZodString) return "string";
 43 |   if (schema instanceof ZodNumber) return "number";
 44 |   if (schema instanceof ZodBoolean) return "boolean";
 45 |   // Extend this function if other Zod types (e.g., ZodEnum, ZodArray) are used in tool parameters
 46 |   return "unknown"; // Fallback for unhandled Zod types
 47 | }
 48 | 
 49 | /**
 50 |  * Serializes the parameters of a tool, expecting a ZodObject schema.
 51 |  * @param zodSchema The ZodObject schema for the tool's parameters.
 52 |  * @returns A serialized representation of the parameters.
 53 |  */
 54 | function serializeParameters(
 55 |   zodSchema: ZodTypeAny
 56 | ): SerializedParameters | { error: string; typeReceived?: string } {
 57 |   // Handle undefined or null schema
 58 |   if (!zodSchema) {
 59 |     return {
 60 |       error: "Parameters schema is undefined or null",
 61 |     };
 62 |   }
 63 | 
 64 |   // Handle non-ZodObject schemas
 65 |   if (!(zodSchema instanceof ZodObject)) {
 66 |     // If it's a primitive type, wrap it in an object
 67 |     if (
 68 |       zodSchema instanceof ZodString ||
 69 |       zodSchema instanceof ZodNumber ||
 70 |       zodSchema instanceof ZodBoolean
 71 |     ) {
 72 |       return {
 73 |         value: {
 74 |           type: getParameterType(zodSchema),
 75 |           description: zodSchema.description,
 76 |         },
 77 |       };
 78 |     }
 79 | 
 80 |     // For other types, return an error
 81 |     return {
 82 |       error: "Parameters schema is not a ZodObject as expected.",
 83 |       typeReceived: zodSchema._def?.typeName || "unknown",
 84 |     };
 85 |   }
 86 | 
 87 |   const paramsShape = zodSchema.shape;
 88 |   const serializedParams: SerializedParameters = {};
 89 | 
 90 |   for (const key in paramsShape) {
 91 |     let currentFieldSchema: ZodSchema = paramsShape[key];
 92 |     const fieldDetails: Partial<SerializedParameter> = {};
 93 |     let isOptional = false;
 94 | 
 95 |     // Check if the field is optional or has a default value, and unwrap it
 96 |     if (currentFieldSchema instanceof ZodOptional) {
 97 |       isOptional = true;
 98 |       currentFieldSchema = currentFieldSchema.unwrap();
 99 |     } else if (currentFieldSchema instanceof ZodDefault) {
100 |       isOptional = true; // Default implies optional for input filling purposes
101 |       currentFieldSchema = currentFieldSchema.removeDefault();
102 |     }
103 | 
104 |     fieldDetails.type = getParameterType(currentFieldSchema);
105 |     if (currentFieldSchema.description) {
106 |       fieldDetails.description = currentFieldSchema.description;
107 |     }
108 |     if (isOptional) {
109 |       fieldDetails.optional = true;
110 |     }
111 | 
112 |     serializedParams[key] = fieldDetails as unknown as SerializedParameter;
113 |   }
114 |   return serializedParams;
115 | }
116 | 
117 | // Write the data to mcptools.json
118 | const MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH = join(process.cwd(), "mcptools.json");
119 | async function getExistingTools() {
120 |   try {
121 |     const content = await readFile(MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH, "utf8");
122 |     if (!content.trim()) {
123 |       return { mcpServers: {} };
124 |     }
125 |     return JSON.parse(content);
126 |   } catch {
127 |     return { mcpServers: {} };
128 |   }
129 | }
130 | 
131 | /**
132 |  * GET handler for the /api/tools route.
133 |  * Serializes and returns the definitions of tools from lib/tools.ts.
134 |  */
135 | export async function GET() {
136 |   try {
137 |     const { tools, breakdown, closeClients } = await getTools();
138 |     await closeClients();
139 |     const serializedTools: Record<string, SerializedTool> = {};
140 | 
141 |     for (const [name, toolInstance] of Object.entries(tools)) {
142 |       try {
143 |         serializedTools[name] = {
144 |           description: toolInstance.description,
145 |           parameters: serializeParameters(toolInstance.parameters),
146 |         };
147 |       } catch (error) {
148 |         console.error(`Error serializing tool ${name}:`, error);
149 |         serializedTools[name] = {
150 |           description: toolInstance.description,
151 |           parameters: {
152 |             error: `Failed to serialize parameters for tool ${name}`,
153 |           },
154 |         };
155 |       }
156 |     }
157 | 
158 |     return NextResponse.json({
159 |       tools: serializedTools,
160 |       breakdown,
161 |       config: await getExistingTools(),
162 |     });
163 |   } catch (error) {
164 |     console.error("Error serializing tools:", error);
165 |     return NextResponse.json(
166 |       { error: "Failed to serialize tools" },
167 |       { status: 500 }
168 |     );
169 |   }
170 | }
171 | 
172 | export async function POST(request: Request) {
173 |   try {
174 |     const data = await request.json();
175 | 
176 |     console.log("DATA", data);
177 | 
178 |     // Validate that we received valid JSON data
179 |     if (!data || typeof data !== "object") {
180 |       return NextResponse.json(
181 |         { error: "Invalid JSON payload" },
182 |         { status: 400 }
183 |       );
184 |     }
185 | 
186 |     let existingTools: { mcpServers: Record<string, unknown> } = {
187 |       mcpServers: {},
188 |     };
189 |     try {
190 |       existingTools = await getExistingTools();
191 |     } catch {
192 |       console.log("MCP tools file doesn't exist, creating it");
193 |       await writeFile(MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH, "{}");
194 |     }
195 | 
196 |     const writing = JSON.stringify(
197 |       {
198 |         mcpServers: {
199 |           ...(existingTools.mcpServers || {}),
200 |           ...data.mcpServers,
201 |         },
202 |       },
203 |       null,
204 |       2
205 |     );
206 |     console.log("WITH API", process.env.BROWSERBASE_API_KEY, writing);
207 |     await writeFile(MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH, writing);
208 | 
209 |     return NextResponse.json(
210 |       { message: "Tools data saved successfully" },
211 |       { status: 200 }
212 |     );
213 |   } catch (error) {
214 |     console.error("Error saving tools data:", error);
215 |     return NextResponse.json(
216 |       { error: "Failed to save tools data" },
217 |       { status: 500 }
218 |     );
219 |   }
220 | }
221 | 
222 | export async function DELETE() {
223 |   try {
224 |     // Attempt to delete the mcptools.json file
225 |     await unlink(MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH);
226 |     return NextResponse.json(
227 |       { message: "mcptools.json deleted successfully" },
228 |       { status: 200 }
229 |     );
230 |   } catch (error: unknown) {
231 |     // If the file does not exist, treat as success
232 |     if (error instanceof Error && error.message.includes("ENOENT")) {
233 |       return NextResponse.json(
234 |         { message: "mcptools.json did not exist, nothing to delete" },
235 |         { status: 200 }
236 |       );
237 |     }
238 |     console.error("Error deleting mcptools.json:", error);
239 |     return NextResponse.json(
240 |       { error: "Failed to delete mcptools.json" },
241 |       { status: 500 }
242 |     );
243 |   }
244 | }
245 |

  1 | "use client";
  2 | 
  3 | import type React from "react";
  4 | import { Message, useChat } from "@ai-sdk/react";

  6 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";

  9 | import { Send, Square } from "lucide-react";
 10 | import { LoadingMessage } from "@/components/loading-message";
 11 | import { useEffect, useCallback, useRef } from "react";
 12 | // ShadCN Sidebar components - Assuming this is the correct path
 13 | import {
 14 |   Sidebar,
 15 |   SidebarHeader,
 16 |   SidebarContent,
 17 |   SidebarGroup,
 18 |   SidebarProvider,
 19 | } from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
 20 | import { useAtom, useAtomValue, useSetAtom } from "jotai/react";
 21 | import {
 22 |   commitHeadAtom,
 23 |   commitsAtom,
 24 |   commitThreadAtom,
 25 |   currentCommitChildrenAtom,
 26 |   currentCommitChildrenIndexMapAtom,
 27 |   fullCommitListAtom,
 28 |   isLoadingAtom,
 29 |   lastUserCommitAtom,
 30 | } from "@/services/gitchat/atoms";
 31 | import {
 32 |   cmdkOpenAtom,
 33 |   dialogOpenAtom,
 34 |   pendingMessageConfigAtom,
 35 | } from "@/services/commands/atoms";
 36 | import { Export } from "@/components/export";
 37 | import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
 38 | import { CmdK } from "@/components/cmdk";
 39 | import gitChat from "@/services/gitchat/client";
 40 | import type { GitChat, Commit } from "@/services/gitchat/client";
 41 | import { ToolsSidebar } from "@/components/tools-sidebar";
 42 | import Keybinding from "@/components/keybinding";
 43 | import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 44 | import { ServerConfigDialog } from "@/components/server-config-dialog";
 45 | import { breakdownAtom, isMcpConfigOpenAtom } from "@/services/mcp/atoms";
 46 | 
 47 | // Function to format date into a pretty relative time
 48 | const formatRelativeTime = (dateString: string): string => {
 49 |   const date = new Date(dateString);
 50 |   const now = new Date();
 51 |   const diffInSeconds = Math.floor((now.getTime() - date.getTime()) / 1000);
 52 | 
 53 |   if (diffInSeconds < 60) {
 54 |     return `${diffInSeconds}s`;
 55 |   } else if (diffInSeconds < 3600) {
 56 |     return `${Math.floor(diffInSeconds / 60)}m`;
 57 |   } else if (diffInSeconds < 86400) {
 58 |     return `${Math.floor(diffInSeconds / 3600)}h`;
 59 |   } else {
 60 |     return `${Math.floor(diffInSeconds / 86400)}d`;
 61 |   }
 62 | };
 63 | 
 64 | export default function ChatPage() {
 65 |   // Ref for the scroll viewport
 66 |   const scrollAreaRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
 67 |   // Ref for the input field
 68 |   const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement | null>(null);
 69 | 
 70 |   // GitChat instance
 71 |   const chatRef = useRef<GitChat>(null);
 72 |   useEffect(() => {
 73 |     if (!chatRef.current) {
 74 |       chatRef.current = gitChat;
 75 |     }
 76 |   }, []);
 77 | 
 78 |   // Atoms
 79 |   const commitHead = useAtomValue(commitHeadAtom);
 80 |   const commits = useAtomValue(commitsAtom);
 81 |   const commitThread = useAtomValue(commitThreadAtom);
 82 |   const fullCommitList = useAtomValue(fullCommitListAtom);
 83 |   const pendingMessageConfig = useAtomValue(pendingMessageConfigAtom);
 84 |   const currentCommitChildren = useAtomValue(currentCommitChildrenAtom);
 85 |   const currentCommitChildrenIndexMap = useAtomValue(
 86 |     currentCommitChildrenIndexMapAtom
 87 |   );
 88 |   const lastUserCommit = useAtomValue(lastUserCommitAtom);
 89 |   const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useAtom(isLoadingAtom);
 90 |   const [cmdkOpen, setCmdkOpen] = useAtom(cmdkOpenAtom);
 91 |   const setDialogOpen = useSetAtom(dialogOpenAtom);
 92 |   const setMcpConfigOpen = useSetAtom(isMcpConfigOpenAtom);
 93 |   const breakdown = useAtomValue(breakdownAtom);
 94 | 
 95 |   useEffect(() => {
 96 |     if (breakdown) {
 97 |       console.log("Breakdown:", breakdown);
 98 |     }
 99 |   }, [breakdown]);
100 | 
101 |   const messageFinishCallback = useCallback(
102 |     (assistantMessage: Message) => {
103 |       console.debug("FINISH - AI Message:", assistantMessage);
104 |       if (chatRef.current && assistantMessage.role === "assistant") {
105 |         // The 'commitHead' atom at this point should be the ID of the user's message
106 |         // that initiated this turn, because we set it at the end of onSubmit.
107 |         // To ensure we get the latest value and avoid stale closures,
108 |         // read directly from the store. By the time onFinish is called,
109 |         // onSubmit should have updated commitHeadAtom to the user's message ID.
110 |         const parentOfAssistantMessage = chatRef.current?.commitHead;
111 | 
112 |         const aiCommit: Commit = {
113 |           id: assistantMessage.id,
114 |           message: assistantMessage.content,
115 |           author:
116 |             assistantMessage.role === "assistant"
117 |               ? pendingMessageConfig.modelName
118 |               : "user",
119 |           date: (assistantMessage.createdAt ?? new Date()).toISOString(),
120 |           metadata: { message: assistantMessage },
121 |           parentId: parentOfAssistantMessage ?? undefined, // Parent is the user commit
122 |         };
123 |         chatRef.current?.addCommit(aiCommit, true);
124 |         chatRef.current?.setCommitHead(aiCommit.id); // Update global commit head to this new AI commit
125 |         setIsLoading(false);
126 |       }
127 |     },
128 |     [pendingMessageConfig.modelName, setIsLoading]
129 |   );
130 | 
131 |   const { messages, status, input, setInput, setMessages, append, stop } =
132 |     useChat({
133 |       id: commitHead ?? undefined,
134 |       body: {
135 |         pendingMessageConfig,
136 |       },
137 |       onToolCall: (arg) => {
138 |         console.debug("TOOL CALL", arg);
139 |       },
140 |       onFinish: messageFinishCallback,
141 |       onResponse: (arg) => {
142 |         console.debug("RESPONSE", arg);
143 |       },
144 |       onError: (arg) => {
145 |         console.debug("ERROR", arg);
146 |       },
147 |     });
148 | 
149 |   useEffect(() => {
150 |     if (status === "submitted" || status === "streaming") {
151 |       setIsLoading(true);
152 |     } else {
153 |       setIsLoading(false);
154 |     }
155 |   }, [status, setIsLoading]);
156 | 
157 |   const onSubmit = useCallback(
158 |     (e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) => {
159 |       e.preventDefault();
160 |       if (input.trim()) {
161 |         setIsLoading(true);
162 |         const message: Message = {
163 |           id: crypto.randomUUID(),
164 |           content: input,
165 |           role: "user",
166 |           createdAt: new Date(),
167 |         };
168 |         const commit: Commit = {
169 |           id: message.id,
170 |           message: message.content,
171 |           author: message.role,
172 |           date:
173 |             message.createdAt instanceof Date
174 |               ? message.createdAt.toISOString()
175 |               : new Date().toISOString(),
176 |           metadata: {
177 |             message,
178 |           },
179 |           parentId: chatRef.current?.commitHead,
180 |         };
181 |         setInput("");
182 |         chatRef.current?.addCommit(commit, true);
183 |         chatRef.current?.setCommitHead(commit.id);
184 |         append(commit.metadata.message);
185 |       }
186 |     },
187 |     [input, setInput, append, setIsLoading]
188 |   );
189 | 
190 |   // Auto-scroll to bottom when messages change
191 |   useEffect(() => {
192 |     const viewport = scrollAreaRef.current?.querySelector(
193 |       "[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]"
194 |     );
195 |     if (viewport) {
196 |       viewport.scrollTop = viewport.scrollHeight;
197 |     }
198 |   }, [messages]);
199 | 
200 |   // Set the messages to the commit thread when the commit thread changes
201 |   useEffect(() => {
202 |     setMessages(commitThread.map((c) => c.metadata.message));
203 |   }, [commitThread, setMessages]);
204 | 
205 |   // Effect to focus input on Tab key press
206 |   useEffect(() => {
207 |     const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
208 |       if (event.key === "Escape") {
209 |         inputRef.current?.blur();
210 |       }
211 |       // If the input is focused, don't do anything
212 |       if (document.activeElement === inputRef.current) return;
213 |       if (event.key === "Tab" || event.key === "i") {
214 |         event.preventDefault();
215 |         inputRef.current?.focus();
216 |       }
217 | 
218 |       if (event.key === "k" && (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)) {
219 |         event.preventDefault();
220 |         setCmdkOpen((open) => !open);
221 |       }
222 | 
223 |       // If there's a message streaming, pause all key presses below this
224 |       if (isLoading || cmdkOpen) return;
225 |       console.log("event.key", event.key, isLoading, cmdkOpen);
226 | 
227 |       // Clear the chat (start a new thread)
228 |       if (event.key === "c") {
229 |         event.preventDefault();
230 |         chatRef.current?.clearCommits();
231 |       }
232 | 
233 |       // Configure MCP
234 |       if (event.key === "m") {
235 |         event.preventDefault();
236 |         setMcpConfigOpen(true);
237 |       }
238 | 
239 |       // Configure Exports
240 |       if (event.key === "e") {
241 |         event.preventDefault();
242 |         setDialogOpen(true);
243 |       }
244 | 
245 |       if (commitHead) {
246 |         const commit = commits[commitHead];
247 |         // Go to the last user commit
248 |         if (event.key === "u") {
249 |           event.preventDefault();
250 |           chatRef.current?.redoLastUserCommit();
251 |         }
252 | 
253 |         // Retry the last user message
254 |         if (event.key === "r") {
255 |           if (commit.metadata.message.content) {
256 |             setIsLoading(true);
257 |             append(commit.metadata.message);
258 |           }
259 |         }
260 | 
261 |         // Go to the previous message
262 |         if (event.key === "p") {
263 |           event.preventDefault();
264 |           if (commit.parentId) {
265 |             chatRef.current?.setCommitHead(commit.parentId);
266 |           }
267 |         }
268 | 
269 |         // Go to the child node at the specified index in currentCommitChildren
270 |         if (!isNaN(Number(event.key)) && event.key.trim() !== "") {
271 |           const index = Number(event.key);
272 |           if (index > 0 && index <= currentCommitChildren.length) {
273 |             chatRef.current?.setCommitHead(currentCommitChildren[index - 1].id);
274 |           }
275 |         }
276 |       }
277 |     };
278 | 
279 |     document.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
280 | 
281 |     // Cleanup function to remove the event listener
282 |     return () => {
283 |       document.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
284 |     };
285 |   }, [
286 |     commitHead,
287 |     commits,
288 |     currentCommitChildren,
289 |     setCmdkOpen,
290 |     isLoading,
291 |     cmdkOpen,
292 |     setMcpConfigOpen,
293 |     setDialogOpen,
294 |   ]);
295 | 
296 |   return (
297 |     <SidebarProvider>
298 |       <div className="flex flex-row h-screen w-full">
299 |         {/* Left Sidebar */}
300 |         <Sidebar className="border-r flex flex-col">
301 |           <SidebarHeader className="py-4">
302 |             <Button
303 |               variant="outline"
304 |               size="sm"
305 |               onClick={() => {
306 |                 chatRef.current?.clearCommits(true);
307 |               }}
308 |             >
309 |               Clear
310 |             </Button>
311 |           </SidebarHeader>
312 |           <SidebarContent className="flex-grow overflow-y-auto">
313 |             <SidebarGroup className="py-2 px-0">
314 |               {fullCommitList.map((commit) => {
315 |                 // Determine background color based on commit selection and parent relationship
316 |                 let bgColor = "";
317 |                 if (commitHead === commit.id) {
318 |                   // Current commit head
319 |                   bgColor = "bg-primary/10 dark:bg-muted py-6";
320 |                 }
321 |                 let author = <span>{commit.author}</span>;
322 |                 if (currentCommitChildrenIndexMap[commit.id] !== undefined) {
323 |                   author = (
324 |                     <div className="my-2">
325 |                       <Keybinding>
326 |                         {currentCommitChildrenIndexMap[commit.id] + 1}
327 |                       </Keybinding>{" "}
328 |                       <span className="ml-2 font-bold">Next user message</span>
329 |                     </div>
330 |                   );
331 |                 }
332 |                 if (
333 |                   commitHead !== null &&
334 |                   commit.id === commits[commitHead]?.parentId
335 |                 ) {
336 |                   author = (
337 |                     <div className="my-2">
338 |                       <Keybinding>P</Keybinding>{" "}
339 |                       <span className="ml-2 font-bold">Previous message</span>
340 |                     </div>
341 |                   );
342 |                 }
343 |                 return (
344 |                   <div
345 |                     key={commit.id}
346 |                     onClick={() => {
347 |                       if (isLoading) return;
348 |                       chatRef.current?.setCommitHead(commit.id);
349 |                       setMessages(commitThread.map((c) => c.metadata.message));
350 |                     }}
351 |                     className={cn(
352 |                       `px-4 py-3 rounded-md ${bgColor}`,
353 |                       isLoading
354 |                         ? "cursor-default"
355 |                         : "cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-muted"
356 |                     )}
357 |                   >
358 |                     <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
359 |                       <span className="text-muted-foreground">{author}</span>
360 |                       <span>
361 |                         <span
362 |                           className="font-semibold"
363 |                           suppressHydrationWarning={true}
364 |                         >
365 |                           {formatRelativeTime(commit.date)}
366 |                         </span>
367 |                         {" · "}
368 |                         <Badge variant="outline" className="mx-1">
369 |                           {commit.id.slice(0, 10)}
370 |                         </Badge>
371 |                       </span>
372 |                       <span
373 |                         className="text-foreground truncate"
374 |                         style={{
375 |                           maxWidth: "100%",
376 |                           overflow: "hidden",
377 |                           textOverflow: "ellipsis",
378 |                           whiteSpace: "nowrap",
379 |                           display: "block",
380 |                         }}
381 |                         title={commit.message}
382 |                       >
383 |                         {commit.message}
384 |                       </span>
385 |                     </div>
386 |                   </div>
387 |                 );
388 |               })}
389 |             </SidebarGroup>
390 |           </SidebarContent>
391 |         </Sidebar>
392 | 
393 |         {/* Main Chat Content */}
394 |         <div className="flex flex-col flex-1 h-full overflow-x-auto">
395 |           <header className="p-4 border-b flex justify-between items-center">
396 |             <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold">Git Chat</h1>
397 |           </header>
398 | 
399 |           <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4 space-y-4" ref={scrollAreaRef}>
400 |             <div className="max-w-xs lg:max-w-3xl mx-auto space-y-4 pb-20">
401 |               {commitThread.length === 0 &&
402 |               !isLoading &&
403 |               currentCommitChildren.length === 0 ? (
404 |                 <div className="text-center py-20 flex flex-col items-center gap-4">
405 |                   <span className="text-muted-foreground">
406 |                     <span className="text-xl text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2 justify-center">
407 |                       Press{" "}
408 |                       <kbd className="pointer-events-none inline-flex h-5 select-none items-center gap-1 rounded border bg-muted px-1.5 font-mono text-[10px] font-medium text-muted-foreground opacity-100">
409 |                         Tab
410 |                       </kbd>{" "}
411 |                       to type a message.
412 |                     </span>
413 |                   </span>
414 |                   <span className="text-muted-foreground">
415 |                     <span className="text-xl text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2 justify-center">
416 |                       <kbd className="pointer-events-none inline-flex h-5 select-none items-center gap-1 rounded border bg-muted px-1.5 font-mono text-[10px] font-medium text-muted-foreground opacity-100">
417 |                         <span className="text-xs">⌘</span>K
418 |                       </kbd>{" "}
419 |                       to open the command palette.
420 |                     </span>
421 |                   </span>
422 |                 </div>
423 |               ) : (
424 |                 commitThread.map((commit, index) => (
425 |                   <div key={`msg-${commit.id}-${index}`}>
426 |                     <div className="w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
427 |                       <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
428 |                         {commit.author}
429 |                       </p>
430 |                       <p
431 |                         className="text-xs text-muted-foreground"
432 |                         suppressHydrationWarning={true}
433 |                       >
434 |                         {formatRelativeTime(commit.date)}
435 |                       </p>
436 |                       <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
437 |                         <Badge variant="outline">
438 |                           {commit.id.slice(0, 10)}
439 |                         </Badge>
440 |                       </p>
441 |                     </div>
442 |                     <ChatMessage commit={commit} />
443 |                     <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
444 |                       {lastUserCommit?.id === commit.id && !isLoading && (
445 |                         <>
446 |                           <Button
447 |                             variant="ghost"
448 |                             size="sm"
449 |                             onClick={() =>
450 |                               chatRef.current?.redoLastUserCommit()
451 |                             }
452 |                           >
453 |                             <Keybinding>U</Keybinding> Undo
454 |                           </Button>
455 |                           <Button
456 |                             variant="ghost"
457 |                             size="sm"
458 |                             onClick={() => {
459 |                               if (commit.metadata.message.content) {
460 |                                 setIsLoading(true);
461 |                                 append(commit.metadata.message);
462 |                               }
463 |                             }}
464 |                           >
465 |                             <Keybinding>R</Keybinding> Retry
466 |                           </Button>
467 |                         </>
468 |                       )}
469 |                     </div>
470 |                   </div>
471 |                 ))
472 |               )}
473 |               {status === "streaming" && (
474 |                 <ChatMessage
475 |                   commit={commitThread[commitThread.length - 1]}
476 |                   messageProp={messages[messages.length - 1]}
477 |                 />
478 |               )}
479 |               {isLoading && <LoadingMessage />}
480 |               {currentCommitChildren.length > 0 && (
481 |                 <ScrollArea className="max-w-3xl whitespace-nowrap rounded-md border">
482 |                   <div className="flex w-max space-x-4 p-4">
483 |                     {currentCommitChildren.map((commit) => {
484 |                       // Determine background color based on commit selection and parent relationship
485 |                       let bgColor = "";
486 |                       if (commitHead === commit.id) {
487 |                         // Current commit head
488 |                         bgColor = "bg-gray-200 dark:bg-muted py-6";
489 |                       } else if (
490 |                         commitHead &&
491 |                         commits[commitHead]?.parentId === commit.id
492 |                       ) {
493 |                         // This commit is the parent of the current head
494 |                         // TODO: Add a different color for this
495 |                       } else if (
496 |                         commit.parentId &&
497 |                         commit.parentId === commitHead
498 |                       ) {
499 |                         // This commit is a child of the current head
500 |                         bgColor =
501 |                           "border-1 border-dashed border-gray-400 dark:border-gray-500/50";
502 |                       }
503 |                       return (
504 |                         <div
505 |                           key={commit.id}
506 |                           onClick={() => {
507 |                             chatRef.current?.setCommitHead(commit.id);
508 |                             setMessages(
509 |                               commitThread.map((c) => c.metadata.message)
510 |                             );
511 |                           }}
512 |                           className={`cursor-pointer px-4 py-3 hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-muted rounded-md ${bgColor} w-64`}
513 |                         >
514 |                           <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
515 |                             <span className="text-muted-foreground truncate">
516 |                               {currentCommitChildrenIndexMap[commit.id] !==
517 |                                 undefined && (
518 |                                 <Keybinding>
519 |                                   {currentCommitChildrenIndexMap[commit.id] + 1}
520 |                                 </Keybinding>
521 |                               )}
522 |                               <span className="ml-2">{commit.author}</span>
523 |                             </span>
524 |                             <span>
525 |                               <span
526 |                                 className="font-semibold"
527 |                                 suppressHydrationWarning={true}
528 |                               >
529 |                                 {formatRelativeTime(commit.date)}
530 |                               </span>
531 |                               {" · "}
532 |                               <Badge variant="outline" className="mx-1">
533 |                                 {commit.id.slice(0, 10)}
534 |                               </Badge>
535 |                             </span>
536 |                             <span
537 |                               className="text-foreground truncate"
538 |                               style={{
539 |                                 maxWidth: "100%",
540 |                                 overflow: "hidden",
541 |                                 textOverflow: "ellipsis",
542 |                                 whiteSpace: "nowrap",
543 |                                 display: "block",
544 |                               }}
545 |                               title={commit.message}
546 |                             >
547 |                               {commit.message}
548 |                             </span>
549 |                           </div>
550 |                         </div>
551 |                       );
552 |                     })}
553 |                   </div>
554 |                   <ScrollBar orientation="horizontal" />
555 |                 </ScrollArea>
556 |               )}
557 |             </div>
558 |           </ScrollArea>
559 | 
560 |           <div className="p-4 border-t">
561 |             <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
562 |               <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-2 gap-4">
563 |                 <div>
564 |                   <h1 className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
565 |                     Model: {pendingMessageConfig.modelName}
566 |                   </h1>
567 |                 </div>
568 |                 <div className="flex gap-2">
569 |                   <ServerConfigDialog />
570 |                   <Button
571 |                     variant="outline"
572 |                     size="sm"
573 |                     onClick={() => setMcpConfigOpen(true)}
574 |                   >
575 |                     <Keybinding>M</Keybinding> MCP
576 |                   </Button>
577 |                   {commitThread.length > 0 && (
578 |                     <>
579 |                       <Export />
580 |                       <Button
581 |                         variant="outline"
582 |                         size="sm"
583 |                         onClick={() => setDialogOpen(true)}
584 |                       >
585 |                         <Keybinding>E</Keybinding> Export Chat
586 |                       </Button>
587 |                       {!isLoading && (
588 |                         <Button
589 |                           variant="outline"
590 |                           size="sm"
591 |                           onClick={() => {
592 |                             chatRef.current?.clearCommits();
593 |                           }}
594 |                         >
595 |                           <Keybinding>C</Keybinding> New Thread
596 |                         </Button>
597 |                       )}
598 |                     </>
599 |                   )}
600 |                 </div>
601 |               </div>
602 |               <form onSubmit={onSubmit} className="flex gap-2">
603 |                 <Input
604 |                   ref={inputRef}
605 |                   value={input}
606 |                   onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
607 |                   placeholder="[PRESS TAB] Type a message..."
608 |                   className="flex-1"
609 |                   disabled={isLoading}
610 |                   autoFocus
611 |                 />
612 |                 {status === "streaming" ? (
613 |                   <Button
614 |                     type="button"
615 |                     className="bg-red-500"
616 |                     size="icon"
617 |                     onClick={() => stop()}
618 |                   >
619 |                     <Square className="h-4 w-4" />
620 |                   </Button>
621 |                 ) : (
622 |                   <Button
623 |                     type="submit"
624 |                     size="icon"
625 |                     disabled={isLoading || !input.trim()}
626 |                   >
627 |                     <Send className="h-4 w-4" />
628 |                   </Button>
629 |                 )}
630 |                 <CmdK />
631 |               </form>
632 |             </div>
633 |           </div>
634 |         </div>
635 | 
636 |         {/* Tools Sidebar on the right */}
637 |         <ToolsSidebar />
638 |       </div>
639 |     </SidebarProvider>
640 |   );
641 | }

  1 | "use client";
  2 | 
  3 | import { useChat } from "@ai-sdk/react";
  4 | import { MemoizedMarkdown } from "./memoized-markdown";
  5 | import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  6 | import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
  7 | import Image from "next/image";
  8 | import { Square, FileJson, FileText, Copy, Download } from "lucide-react";
  9 | import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
 10 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 11 | import {
 12 |   Dialog,
 13 |   DialogContent,
 14 |   DialogHeader,
 15 |   DialogTitle,
 16 |   DialogTrigger,
 17 |   DialogFooter,
 18 | } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 19 | import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
 20 | import type { Message } from "@ai-sdk/react";
 21 | 
 22 | type MessagePart = {
 23 |   type: string;
 24 |   text?: string;
 25 |   toolInvocation?: {
 26 |     toolName: string;
 27 |     state: string;
 28 |     args?: Record<string, unknown>;
 29 |   };
 30 | };
 31 | 
 32 | export default function ChatCompletion() {
 33 |   const { messages, append, setInput, input, status, stop } = useChat({
 34 |     onToolCall: (arg) => {
 35 |       console.debug("TOOL CALL", arg, messages);
 36 |     },
 37 |     onFinish: (arg) => {
 38 |       console.debug("FINISH", arg, messages);
 39 |       setLoading(false);
 40 |     },
 41 |     onResponse: (arg) => {
 42 |       console.debug("RESPONSE", arg, messages);
 43 |     },
 44 |     onError: (arg) => {
 45 |       console.debug("ERROR", arg, messages);
 46 |       setLoading(false);
 47 |     },
 48 |   });
 49 |   const hasAppended = useRef(false);
 50 |   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
 51 |   const [messageParts, setMessageParts] = useState<MessagePart[]>([]);
 52 |   const [stoppable, setStoppable] = useState(false);
 53 |   const chatContainerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
 54 |   const scrollAreaRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
 55 |   const [showTranscriptModal, setShowTranscriptModal] = useState(false);
 56 |   const [transcriptContent, setTranscriptContent] = useState("");
 57 |   const [transcriptFormat, setTranscriptFormat] = useState<"json" | "markdown">(
 58 |     "json"
 59 |   );
 60 | 
 61 |   const formatToJson = (msgs: Message[]): string => {
 62 |     return JSON.stringify(msgs, null, 2);
 63 |   };
 64 | 
 65 |   const formatToMarkdown = (msgs: Message[]): string => {
 66 |     return msgs
 67 |       .map((msg) => {
 68 |         let content = "";
 69 |         if (msg.content) {
 70 |           content = msg.content;
 71 |         } else if (msg.parts) {
 72 |           content = msg.parts
 73 |             .map((part) => {
 74 |               if (part.type === "text") return part.text;
 75 |               if (part.type === "tool-invocation") {
 76 |                 return `*[Tool call: ${part.toolInvocation.toolName} (${
 77 |                   part.toolInvocation.state
 78 |                 })]*\\nArgs: \`\`\`json\\n${JSON.stringify(
 79 |                   part.toolInvocation.args,
 80 |                   null,
 81 |                   2
 82 |                 )}\\n\`\`\` ${
 83 |                   part.toolInvocation.state === "result"
 84 |                     ? `\\nResult: \`\`\`json\\n${JSON.stringify(
 85 |                         part.toolInvocation.result,
 86 |                         null,
 87 |                         2
 88 |                       )}\\n\`\`\``
 89 |                     : ""
 90 |                 }`;
 91 |               }
 92 |               return "";
 93 |             })
 94 |             .join("\\n");
 95 |         }
 96 |         return `**${msg.role === "user" ? "User" : "Assistant"}**: ${content}`;
 97 |       })
 98 |       .join("\\n\\n---\\n\\n");
 99 |   };
100 | 
101 |   useEffect(() => {
102 |     console.debug("STATUS", status);
103 |     setLoading(messages.length === 0 || status !== "ready");
104 |     setStoppable(
105 |       messages[messages.length - 1]?.parts?.filter(
106 |         (p) =>
107 |           p.type === "tool-invocation" && p.toolInvocation.state !== "result"
108 |       ).length === 0
109 |     );
110 |   }, [status, messages]);
111 | 
112 |   useEffect(() => {
113 |     if (!hasAppended.current) {
114 |       hasAppended.current = true;
115 |       setLoading(false);
116 |     }
117 |   }, [append]);
118 | 
119 |   useEffect(() => {
120 |     // Update messageParts when messages change
121 |     const parts = messages.flatMap((message) =>
122 |       message.parts ? message.parts : []
123 |     );
124 |     setMessageParts(parts);
125 |   }, [messages]);
126 | 
127 |   useEffect(() => {
128 |     // Scroll to bottom when messageParts changes
129 |     if (scrollAreaRef.current) {
130 |       const viewport = scrollAreaRef.current.querySelector(
131 |         "[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]"
132 |       );
133 |       if (viewport) {
134 |         viewport.scrollTop = viewport.scrollHeight;
135 |       }
136 |     }
137 |   }, [messageParts]);
138 | 
139 |   const downloadTranscript = () => {
140 |     const mimeType =
141 |       transcriptFormat === "json" ? "application/json" : "text/markdown";
142 |     const filename =
143 |       transcriptFormat === "json"
144 |         ? "chat-transcript.json"
145 |         : "chat-transcript.md";
146 | 
147 |     const blob = new Blob([transcriptContent], { type: mimeType });
148 |     const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
149 |     const a = document.createElement("a");
150 |     a.href = url;
151 |     a.download = filename;
152 |     document.body.appendChild(a);
153 |     a.click();
154 |     document.body.removeChild(a);
155 |     URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
156 |   };
157 | 
158 |   return (
159 |     <div className="h-full w-full flex flex-col justify-between">
160 |       <div className="w-full flex-grow overflow-auto">
161 |         <ScrollArea ref={scrollAreaRef} className="h-full overflow-x-auto">
162 |           <div ref={chatContainerRef} className="h-full pb-4">
163 |             <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 pt-4">
164 |               {messages?.map((message, index) => {
165 |                 if (message.role === "user") {
166 |                   return (
167 |                     <div className="px-4" key={message.id}>
168 |                       <div className="w-full p-4 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-[#635943]/30 to-[#ffdc83]/10">
169 |                         <p className="text-md font-bold font-ppsupply">
170 |                           {message.content.toString()}
171 |                         </p>
172 |                       </div>
173 |                     </div>
174 |                   );
175 |                 }
176 |                 return (
177 |                   <div
178 |                     key={`${message.id}-${index}`}
179 |                     className="flex flex-col gap-4 px-4"
180 |                   >
181 |                     {message.parts.map((part, partIndex) => {
182 |                       if (part.type === "tool-invocation") {
183 |                         const hasIframe = part.toolInvocation.args?.hasIframe;
184 |                         return (
185 |                           <div
186 |                             key={`part-${message.id}-${partIndex}`}
187 |                             className="w-full space-x-2 px-4 py-4 rounded-lg bg-black/80 border border-white/30 overflow-x-auto"
188 |                           >
189 |                             <span
190 |                               className={cn(
191 |                                 "font-bold",
192 |                                 part.toolInvocation.state !== "result" &&
193 |                                   "gradient-background-loading"
194 |                               )}
195 |                             >
196 |                               {part.toolInvocation.toolName.split("_").pop()}{" "}
197 |                               {hasIframe ? " (computer use agent)" : ""}
198 |                             </span>
199 |                             <div className="text-xs">
200 |                               {part.toolInvocation.args &&
201 |                                 Object.entries(part.toolInvocation.args).map(
202 |                                   ([key, value]) => {
203 |                                     return (
204 |                                       <span key={key}>{value as string}</span>
205 |                                     );
206 |                                   }
207 |                                 )}
208 |                             </div>
209 |                             <div className="text-xs">
210 |                               {part.toolInvocation.state === "result" &&
211 |                                 part.toolInvocation.result && (
212 |                                   <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-2">
213 |                                     {part.toolInvocation.toolName ===
214 |                                       "screenshot" ||
215 |                                     part.toolInvocation.toolName ===
216 |                                       "stagehand_act" ? (
217 |                                       <div className="mt-2">
218 |                                         <Image
219 |                                           src={`data:image/png;base64,${part.toolInvocation.result}`}
220 |                                           alt="Screenshot"
221 |                                           width={300}
222 |                                           height={300}
223 |                                           className="max-w-full rounded-lg border border-white/20"
224 |                                         />
225 |                                       </div>
226 |                                     ) : (
227 |                                       <MemoizedMarkdown
228 |                                         id={message.id}
229 |                                         content={part.toolInvocation.result.toString()}
230 |                                       />
231 |                                     )}
232 |                                   </div>
233 |                                 )}
234 |                             </div>
235 |                           </div>
236 |                         );
237 |                       } else if (part.type === "text") {
238 |                         return (
239 |                           <div
240 |                             className="prose prose-invert max-w-none space-y-2 px-4 overflow-x-auto"
241 |                             key={`${message.id}-${partIndex}`}
242 |                           >
243 |                             <MemoizedMarkdown
244 |                               id={message.id}
245 |                               content={part.text.toString()}
246 |                             />
247 |                           </div>
248 |                         );
249 |                       }
250 |                     })}
251 |                     {message.annotations?.map((annotation, annotationIndex) => {
252 |                       if (
253 |                         typeof annotation === "object" &&
254 |                         annotation !== null &&
255 |                         "structuredResult" in annotation
256 |                       ) {
257 |                         return (
258 |                           <div
259 |                             key={`annotation-${message.id}-${annotationIndex}`}
260 |                             className="w-full rounded-lg px-4 py-2 bg-black/30 border border-white/30 overflow-auto flex flex-col gap-2"
261 |                           >
262 |                             <h1 className="font-bold text-lg">Final Result</h1>
263 |                             <pre className="text-xs overflow-x-auto">
264 |                               {JSON.stringify(
265 |                                 annotation.structuredResult,
266 |                                 null,
267 |                                 2
268 |                               )}
269 |                             </pre>
270 |                           </div>
271 |                         );
272 |                       }
273 |                       return <></>;
274 |                     })}
275 |                   </div>
276 |                 );
277 |               })}
278 |             </div>
279 |           </div>
280 |         </ScrollArea>
281 |       </div>
282 |       {/* Transcript Export Buttons and Modal - Improved visibility */}
283 |       {!loading && messages.length > 0 && (
284 |         <Dialog
285 |           open={showTranscriptModal}
286 |           onOpenChange={setShowTranscriptModal}
287 |         >
288 |           <div className="flex justify-end gap-2 p-4 border-t border-white/10">
289 |             <DialogTrigger asChild>
290 |               <Button
291 |                 variant="outline"
292 |                 size="sm"
293 |                 className="flex gap-2 items-center"
294 |                 onClick={() => {
295 |                   setTranscriptFormat("json");
296 |                   setTranscriptContent(formatToJson(messages));
297 |                   setShowTranscriptModal(true);
298 |                 }}
299 |               >
300 |                 <FileJson className="h-4 w-4" />
301 |                 <span>JSON</span>
302 |               </Button>
303 |             </DialogTrigger>
304 |             <DialogTrigger asChild>
305 |               <Button
306 |                 variant="outline"
307 |                 size="sm"
308 |                 className="flex gap-2 items-center"
309 |                 onClick={() => {
310 |                   setTranscriptFormat("markdown");
311 |                   setTranscriptContent(formatToMarkdown(messages));
312 |                   setShowTranscriptModal(true);
313 |                 }}
314 |               >
315 |                 <FileText className="h-4 w-4" />
316 |                 <span>Markdown</span>
317 |               </Button>
318 |             </DialogTrigger>
319 |           </div>
320 |           <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-[600px]">
321 |             <DialogHeader>
322 |               <DialogTitle>
323 |                 Chat Transcript (
324 |                 {transcriptFormat === "json" ? "JSON" : "Markdown"})
325 |               </DialogTitle>
326 |             </DialogHeader>
327 |             <div className="grid gap-4 py-4">
328 |               <Textarea
329 |                 readOnly
330 |                 value={transcriptContent}
331 |                 className="h-[400px] text-xs bg-black/10 dark:bg-white/5"
332 |                 placeholder="Transcript content will appear here..."
333 |               />
334 |             </div>
335 |             <DialogFooter className="flex gap-2">
336 |               <Button
337 |                 variant="outline"
338 |                 className="flex gap-2 items-center"
339 |                 onClick={() => {
340 |                   navigator.clipboard.writeText(transcriptContent);
341 |                 }}
342 |               >
343 |                 <Copy className="h-4 w-4" />
344 |                 <span>Copy</span>
345 |               </Button>
346 |               <Button
347 |                 className="flex gap-2 items-center"
348 |                 onClick={downloadTranscript}
349 |               >
350 |                 <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
351 |                 <span>Download</span>
352 |               </Button>
353 |             </DialogFooter>
354 |           </DialogContent>
355 |         </Dialog>
356 |       )}
357 |       {/* Loading Indicator OR Input Field */}
358 |       {loading ? (
359 |         <div className="flex gap-2 justify-between items-center px-4 pb-4">
360 |           {(stoppable || messages.length === 0) && (
361 |             <button className="flex gap-2 items-center text-md font-bold uppercase gradient-background-loading text-md">
362 |               Loading...
363 |             </button>
364 |           )}
365 |           {stoppable && (
366 |             <div
367 |               className="flex gap-2 items-center border border-white/30 rounded-lg px-3 py-1 bg-black/30"
368 |               onClick={() => stop()}
369 |             >
370 |               <Square className="w-2 h-2 text-transparent bg-white/70" />
371 |               <span className="text-md">Stop</span>
372 |             </div>
373 |           )}
374 |         </div>
375 |       ) : (
376 |         /* Chat Input Field when not loading */
377 |         <div className="flex gap-2 p-4">
378 |           <input
379 |             type="text"
380 |             className="w-full rounded-lg px-4 py-2 bg-black/30 border border-white/30"
381 |             value={input}
382 |             onChange={(event) => {
383 |               setInput(event.target.value);
384 |             }}
385 |             placeholder="Ask a follow up question..."
386 |             autoFocus={true}
387 |             onKeyDown={async (event) => {
388 |               if (event.key === "Enter") {
389 |                 if (input.trim()) {
390 |                   append({ content: input, role: "user" });
391 |                   setInput("");
392 |                 }
393 |               }
394 |             }}
395 |           />
396 |           {messages.length > 0 && (
397 |             <Button
398 |               variant="outline"
399 |               className="flex gap-2 items-center"
400 |               onClick={() => {
401 |                 setTranscriptFormat("json");
402 |                 setTranscriptContent(formatToJson(messages));
403 |                 setShowTranscriptModal(true);
404 |               }}
405 |             >
406 |               <FileText className="h-4 w-4" />
407 |               <span>Export</span>
408 |             </Button>
409 |           )}
410 |         </div>
411 |       )}
412 |     </div>
413 |   );
414 | }

  1 | "use client";
  2 | 
  3 | import * as React from "react";
  4 | 
  5 | import {
  6 |   CommandDialog,
  7 |   CommandEmpty,
  8 |   CommandInput,
  9 |   CommandItem,
 10 |   CommandList,
 11 | } from "@/components/ui/command";
 12 | 
 13 | import {
 14 |   atom,
 15 |   getDefaultStore,
 16 |   useAtom,
 17 |   useAtomValue,
 18 |   useSetAtom,
 19 | } from "jotai";
 20 | import { Command } from "@/services/commands";
 21 | import { atomWithStorage } from "jotai/utils";
 22 | import {
 23 |   cmdkOpenAtom,
 24 |   modelNameAtom,
 25 |   dialogOpenAtom,
 26 | } from "@/services/commands/atoms";
 27 | import { availableModelSchema, type AvailableModel } from "@/sharedTypes";
 28 | import { ChevronRight } from "lucide-react";
 29 | import gitChat from "@/services/gitchat/client";
 30 | import { isMcpLoadingAtom, isMcpConfigOpenAtom } from "@/services/mcp/atoms";
 31 | 
 32 | function setModelName(modelName: AvailableModel) {
 33 |   const store = getDefaultStore();
 34 |   store.set(modelNameAtom, modelName);
 35 | }
 36 | 
 37 | function setMcpConfigOpen(open: boolean) {
 38 |   const store = getDefaultStore();
 39 |   store.set(isMcpConfigOpenAtom, open);
 40 | }
 41 | 
 42 | function setExportDialogOpen(open: boolean) {
 43 |   const store = getDefaultStore();
 44 |   store.set(dialogOpenAtom, open);
 45 | }
 46 | 
 47 | function getIsLoading() {
 48 |   const store = getDefaultStore();
 49 |   return store.get(isMcpLoadingAtom);
 50 | }
 51 | 
 52 | const HIERARCHY_SEPARATOR = " --->>> ";
 53 | 
 54 | const parentIdAtom = atom<string | null>(null);
 55 | const commandTreeAtom = atomWithStorage<Command[]>("commandTree", [
 56 |   {
 57 |     name: "Set Model",
 58 |     id: "set-model",
 59 |   },
 60 |   {
 61 |     name: "MCP Config",
 62 |     id: "mcp-config",
 63 |     onSelect: () => {
 64 |       setMcpConfigOpen(true);
 65 |     },
 66 |   },
 67 |   {
 68 |     name: "Export Chat",
 69 |     id: "export-chat",
 70 |     onSelect: () => {
 71 |       if (!getIsLoading() && gitChat.commitThread.length > 0) {
 72 |         setExportDialogOpen(true);
 73 |       } else {
 74 |         alert("Please wait for the current operation to complete.");
 75 |       }
 76 |     },
 77 |   },
 78 |   {
 79 |     name: "New Thread",
 80 |     id: "new-thread",
 81 |     onSelect: () => {
 82 |       gitChat.clearCommits(true);
 83 |     },
 84 |   },
 85 |   {
 86 |     name: "Search Messages",
 87 |     id: "search-messages",
 88 |   },
 89 |   {
 90 |     name: "DELETE ALL CHATS",
 91 |     id: "delete-all-chats",
 92 |     onSelect: () => {
 93 |       gitChat.clearCommits(true);
 94 |     },
 95 |   },
 96 |   ...availableModelSchema.options.map((model) => ({
 97 |     name: model,
 98 |     id: model,
 99 |     onSelect: () => {
100 |       setModelName(model);
101 |     },
102 |     parentId: "set-model",
103 |   })),
104 |   ...Object.values(gitChat.commits).map((commit) => ({
105 |     name: commit.metadata.message.content,
106 |     id: commit.id,
107 |     onSelect: () => {
108 |       gitChat.setCommitHead(commit.id);
109 |     },
110 |     parentId: "search-messages",
111 |   })),
112 | ]);
113 | 
114 | const commandsListAtom = atom((get) => {
115 |   const commandTree = get(commandTreeAtom);
116 |   const parentId = get(parentIdAtom);
117 |   const commands = commandTree
118 |     .filter((c) => c.parentId === parentId || !parentId)
119 |     .map((command) => {
120 |       const parents = [];
121 |       let node: Command | undefined = command;
122 |       while (node?.parentId) {
123 |         const parent = commandTree.find((c) => c.id === node?.parentId);
124 |         parents.push(parent?.name ?? "");
125 |         node = commandTree.find((c) => c.id === node?.parentId);
126 |       }
127 |       return {
128 |         ...command,
129 |         name:
130 |           parents.reverse().join(HIERARCHY_SEPARATOR) +
131 |           HIERARCHY_SEPARATOR +
132 |           command.name,
133 |       };
134 |     });
135 |   return commands;
136 | });
137 | 
138 | export function CmdK() {
139 |   const [inputValue, setInputValue] = React.useState("");
140 |   const commandsList = useAtomValue(commandsListAtom);
141 |   const setParentId = useSetAtom(parentIdAtom);
142 |   const [open, setOpen] = useAtom(cmdkOpenAtom);
143 | 
144 |   React.useEffect(() => {
145 |     if (!open) {
146 |       setParentId(null);
147 |     }
148 |   }, [open, setParentId]);
149 | 
150 |   return (
151 |     <>
152 |       <CommandDialog open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
153 |         <CommandInput
154 |           placeholder="Type a command or search..."
155 |           value={inputValue}
156 |           onValueChange={setInputValue}
157 |         />
158 |         <CommandList>
159 |           <CommandEmpty>No results found.</CommandEmpty>
160 |           {commandsList.map((command, commandIndex) => {
161 |             return (
162 |               <CommandItem
163 |                 key={`${commandIndex} - ${command.name}`}
164 |                 value={command.name}
165 |                 onSelect={() => {
166 |                   command.onSelect?.();
167 |                   if (command.onSelect) {
168 |                     setOpen(false);
169 |                   } else {
170 |                     setParentId(command.id);
171 |                   }
172 |                 }}
173 |               >
174 |                 {command.name.split(HIERARCHY_SEPARATOR).map((part, index) => {
175 |                   return (
176 |                     <span key={index} className="flex items-center gap-2">
177 |                       {part}
178 |                       {index <
179 |                         command.name.split(HIERARCHY_SEPARATOR).length - 1 && (
180 |                         <ChevronRight />
181 |                       )}
182 |                     </span>
183 |                   );
184 |                 })}
185 |               </CommandItem>
186 |             );
187 |           })}
188 |         </CommandList>
189 |       </CommandDialog>
190 |     </>
191 |   );
192 | }

/components/export.tsx:

 1 | import { FileJson, FileText, Copy } from "lucide-react";
 2 | import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
 3 | import {
 4 |   Dialog,
 5 |   DialogContent,
 6 |   DialogHeader,
 7 |   DialogTitle,
 8 |   DialogFooter,
 9 | } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
10 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
11 | import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from "react";
12 | import { useAtom, useAtomValue } from "jotai/react";
13 | import { commitThreadAtom } from "@/services/gitchat/atoms";
14 | import { dialogOpenAtom } from "@/services/commands/atoms";
15 | import { Commit } from "@/services/gitchat/client";
16 | 
17 | export const Export = () => {
18 |   const [transcriptFormat, setTranscriptFormat] = useState("markdown");
19 |   const [transcriptContent, setTranscriptContent] = useState("");
20 |   const commits = useAtomValue(commitThreadAtom);
21 |   const [dialogOpen, setDialogOpen] = useAtom(dialogOpenAtom);
22 | 
23 |   const formatToJson = useCallback((cms: Commit[]): string => {
24 |     return JSON.stringify(cms, null, 2);
25 |   }, []);
26 | 
27 |   const formatToMarkdown = useCallback((cmts: Commit[]): string => {
28 |     return cmts
29 |       .map((cmt) => {
30 |         return `**${cmt.author}**: ${cmt.message.trim()}`;
31 |       })
32 |       .join("\n\n---\n\n");
33 |   }, []);
34 | 
35 |   useEffect(() => {
36 |     setTranscriptContent(
37 |       transcriptFormat === "json"
38 |         ? formatToJson(commits)
39 |         : formatToMarkdown(commits)
40 |     );
41 |   }, [transcriptFormat, formatToJson, formatToMarkdown, commits]);
42 | 
43 |   return (
44 |     <Dialog open={dialogOpen} onOpenChange={setDialogOpen}>
45 |       <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-[600px]">
46 |         <DialogHeader>
47 |           <DialogTitle>Chat Transcript</DialogTitle>
48 |         </DialogHeader>
49 | 
50 |         <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4 mt-2">
51 |           <div className="flex gap-2">
52 |             <Button
53 |               variant={transcriptFormat === "markdown" ? "default" : "outline"}
54 |               size="sm"
55 |               onClick={() => setTranscriptFormat("markdown")}
56 |             >
57 |               <FileText className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
58 |               Markdown
59 |             </Button>
60 |             <Button
61 |               variant={transcriptFormat === "json" ? "default" : "outline"}
62 |               size="sm"
63 |               onClick={() => setTranscriptFormat("json")}
64 |             >
65 |               <FileJson className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
66 |               JSON
67 |             </Button>
68 |           </div>
69 |         </div>
70 | 
71 |         <Textarea
72 |           readOnly
73 |           value={transcriptContent}
74 |           className="h-[400px] text-xs font-mono"
75 |         />
76 | 
77 |         <DialogFooter className="flex gap-2 mt-4">
78 |           <Button
79 |             variant="outline"
80 |             onClick={() => navigator.clipboard.writeText(transcriptContent)}
81 |           >
82 |             <Copy className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
83 |             Copy
84 |           </Button>
85 |         </DialogFooter>
86 |       </DialogContent>
87 |     </Dialog>
88 |   );
89 | };

/components/keybinding.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | export default function Keybinding({
 2 |   children,
 3 | }: {
 4 |   children: React.ReactNode;
 5 | }) {
 6 |   return (

/components/memoized-markdown.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { Lexer } from "marked";
 2 | import { memo, useMemo } from "react";
 3 | import ReactMarkdown from "react-markdown";
 4 | 
 5 | function parseMarkdownIntoBlocks(markdown: string): string[] {
 6 |   if (typeof markdown !== "string") {
 7 |     throw new Error("Expected markdown to be a string");
 8 |   }
 9 |   const tokens = Lexer.lex(markdown);
10 |   return tokens.map((token) => token.raw);
11 | }
12 | 
13 | const MemoizedMarkdownBlock = memo(
14 |   ({ content }: { content: string }) => {
15 |     return <ReactMarkdown>{content}</ReactMarkdown>;
16 |   },
17 |   (prevProps, nextProps) => {
18 |     if (prevProps.content !== nextProps.content) return false;
19 |     return true;
20 |   }
21 | );
22 | 
23 | MemoizedMarkdownBlock.displayName = "MemoizedMarkdownBlock";
24 | 
25 | export const MemoizedMarkdown = memo(
26 |   ({ content, id }: { content: string; id: string }) => {
27 |     const blocks = useMemo(() => parseMarkdownIntoBlocks(content), [content]);
28 | 
29 |     return blocks.map((block, index) => (
30 |       <MemoizedMarkdownBlock content={block} key={`${id}-block_${index}`} />
31 |     ));
32 |   }
33 | );
34 | 
35 | MemoizedMarkdown.displayName = "MemoizedMarkdown";
36 | 


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/components/message-parser.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | "use client"
 2 | 
 3 | import { useEffect, useState } from "react"
 4 | import type { Message as AIMessage } from "@ai-sdk/react"
 5 | 
 6 | interface ParsedContent {
 7 |   beforeToolCalls: string
 8 |   afterToolCalls: string
 9 | }
10 | 
11 | export function useMessageParser(message: AIMessage): ParsedContent {
12 |   const [parsedContent, setParsedContent] = useState<ParsedContent>({
13 |     beforeToolCalls: message.content || "",
14 |     afterToolCalls: "",
15 |   })
16 | 
17 |   useEffect(() => {
18 |     if (!message.content || !message.toolInvocations?.length) {
19 |       setParsedContent({
20 |         beforeToolCalls: message.content || "",
21 |         afterToolCalls: "",
22 |       })
23 |       return
24 |     }
25 | 
26 |     // In a real implementation, we would use the actual streaming data
27 |     // to determine where tool calls were inserted in the content.
28 |     // For this demo, we'll use a heuristic approach:
29 | 
30 |     // 1. Split the content by common tool call indicators
31 |     const toolCallIndicators = [
32 |       "I'll check that for you",
33 |       "Let me look that up",
34 |       "Let me check",
35 |       "I'll search for",
36 |       "I'll get the weather",
37 |       "I'll find the news",
38 |     ]
39 | 
40 |     let splitIndex = message.content.length
41 | 
42 |     for (const indicator of toolCallIndicators) {
43 |       const index = message.content.indexOf(indicator)
44 |       if (index !== -1 && index < splitIndex) {
45 |         splitIndex = index
46 |       }
47 |     }
48 | 
49 |     // 2. If we found a potential split point, use it
50 |     if (splitIndex < message.content.length) {
51 |       setParsedContent({
52 |         beforeToolCalls: message.content.substring(0, splitIndex).trim(),
53 |         afterToolCalls: message.content.substring(splitIndex).trim(),
54 |       })
55 |     } else {
56 |       // 3. Fallback: assume 70% of content is before tool calls
57 |       const fallbackSplitIndex = Math.floor(message.content.length * 0.7)
58 |       setParsedContent({
59 |         beforeToolCalls: message.content.substring(0, fallbackSplitIndex).trim(),
60 |         afterToolCalls: message.content.substring(fallbackSplitIndex).trim(),
61 |       })
62 |     }
63 |   }, [message.content, message.toolInvocations])
64 | 
65 |   return parsedContent
66 | }
67 |

  1 | import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  2 | import { Avatar } from "@/components/ui/avatar";
  3 | import { User, Bot } from "lucide-react";
  4 | import { MemoizedMarkdown } from "./memoized-markdown";
  5 | import Image from "next/image";
  6 | import {
  7 |   Sheet,
