 14 | import { Commit } from "@/services/gitchat/client";
 15 | import { Message } from "ai";
 16 | 
 17 | export function ChatMessage({
 18 |   commit,
 19 |   messageProp,
 20 | }: {
 21 |   commit: Commit;
 22 |   messageProp?: Message;
 23 | }) {
 24 |   const message = messageProp || commit.metadata.message;
 25 |   const isUser = message.role === "user";
 26 | 
 27 |   // Convert message parts to our MessagePart type
 28 |   const messageParts =
 29 |     message.parts?.map((part) => ({
 30 |       type: part.type,
 31 |       text: part.type === "text" ? part.text : undefined,
 32 |       toolInvocation:
 33 |         part.type === "tool-invocation"
 34 |           ? {
 35 |               toolName: part.toolInvocation.toolName,
 36 |               state: part.toolInvocation.state,
 37 |               args: part.toolInvocation.args,
 38 |               result:
 39 |                 part.toolInvocation.state === "result"
 40 |                   ? part.toolInvocation.result
 41 |                   : undefined,
 42 |             }
 43 |           : undefined,
 44 |     })) || [];
 45 | 
 46 |   return (
 47 |     <div className={cn("flex items-start gap-3", isUser && "flex-row-reverse")}>
 48 |       <Avatar
 49 |         className={cn(
 50 |           "h-8 w-8 mt-0.5 flex items-center justify-center",
 51 |           isUser ? "bg-primary" : "bg-muted"
 52 |         )}
 53 |       >
 54 |         {isUser ? (
 55 |           <User className="h-5 w-5 text-primary-foreground" />
 56 |         ) : (
 57 |           <Bot className="h-5 w-5" />
 58 |         )}
 59 |       </Avatar>
 60 | 
 61 |       <div
 62 |         className={cn(
 63 |           "flex flex-col max-w-[80%] rounded-lg p-4",
 64 |           isUser ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground" : "bg-muted"
 65 |         )}
 66 |       >
 67 |         {isUser ? (
 68 |           <div className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{message.content}</div>
 69 |         ) : (
 70 |           messageParts.map((part, index) => {
 71 |             if (part.type === "tool-invocation" && part.toolInvocation) {
 72 |               const hasIframe = part.toolInvocation.args?.hasIframe;
 73 |               const toolDisplayName = part.toolInvocation.toolName
 74 |                 .split("_")
 75 |                 .pop();
 76 |               return (
 77 |                 <Sheet key={index}>
 78 |                   <SheetTrigger asChild>
 79 |                     <div className="my-3 flex justify-between items-center w-full px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-black/80 border border-white/30 cursor-pointer hover:bg-black/70">
 80 |                       <span
 81 |                         className={cn(
 82 |                           "font-bold text-white",
 83 |                           part.toolInvocation.state !== "result" &&
 84 |                             "gradient-background-loading"
 85 |                         )}
 86 |                       >
 87 |                         {toolDisplayName}{" "}
 88 |                         {hasIframe ? " (computer use agent)" : ""}
 89 |                       </span>
 90 |                     </div>
 91 |                   </SheetTrigger>
 92 |                   <SheetContent
 93 |                     side="right"
 94 |                     className="bg-background text-foreground border-l"
 95 |                   >
 96 |                     <SheetHeader className="mb-4">
 97 |                       <SheetTitle className="text-foreground">
 98 |                         Tool: {toolDisplayName}
 99 |                       </SheetTitle>
100 |                     </SheetHeader>
101 |                     <ScrollArea className="h-[calc(100vh-100px)]">
102 |                       <div className="p-4 rounded-b-lg overflow-x-auto">
103 |                         <div className="text-sm mb-4">
104 |                           <span className="font-semibold block mb-1">
105 |                             Arguments:
106 |                           </span>
107 |                           {part.toolInvocation.args &&
108 |                           Object.entries(part.toolInvocation.args).length >
109 |                             0 ? (
110 |                             Object.entries(part.toolInvocation.args).map(
111 |                               ([key, value]) => (
112 |                                 <div key={key} className="ml-2 mb-1">
113 |                                   <span className="font-medium">{key}:</span>{" "}
114 |                                   <pre className="inline-block bg-muted p-1 rounded text-xs whitespace-pre-wrap text-muted-foreground overflow-x-auto max-w-full">
115 |                                     {JSON.stringify(value, null, 2)}
116 |                                   </pre>
117 |                                 </div>
118 |                               )
119 |                             )
120 |                           ) : (
121 |                             <span className="ml-2 italic">No arguments</span>
122 |                           )}
123 |                         </div>
124 |                         <div className="text-sm">
125 |                           {part.toolInvocation.state === "result" && (
126 |                             <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
127 |                               <span className="font-semibold block mb-1">
128 |                                 Result:
129 |                               </span>
130 |                               {part.toolInvocation.result ? (
131 |                                 <>
132 |                                   {part.toolInvocation.toolName ===
133 |                                     "screenshot" ||
134 |                                   part.toolInvocation.toolName ===
135 |                                     "stagehand_act" ? (
136 |                                     <div className="mt-1 ml-2">
137 |                                       <Image
138 |                                         src={`data:image/png;base64,${part.toolInvocation.result}`}
139 |                                         alt="Screenshot Result"
140 |                                         width={400}
141 |                                         height={400}
142 |                                         className="max-w-full rounded-lg border"
143 |                                       />
144 |                                     </div>
145 |                                   ) : (
146 |                                     <pre className="ml-2 bg-muted p-2 rounded text-muted-foreground overflow-x-auto text-xs whitespace-pre-wrap max-w-full">
147 |                                       {JSON.stringify(
148 |                                         part.toolInvocation.result,
149 |                                         null,
150 |                                         2
151 |                                       )}
152 |                                     </pre>
153 |                                   )}
154 |                                 </>
155 |                               ) : (
156 |                                 <span className="ml-2 italic">
157 |                                   No result data
158 |                                 </span>
159 |                               )}
160 |                             </div>
161 |                           )}
162 |                           {part.toolInvocation.state !== "result" && (
163 |                             <span className="ml-2 italic">
164 |                               Awaiting result...
165 |                             </span>
166 |                           )}
167 |                         </div>
168 |                       </div>
169 |                     </ScrollArea>
170 |                   </SheetContent>
171 |                 </Sheet>
172 |               );
173 |             } else if (part.type === "text" && part.text) {
174 |               const textContent =
175 |                 typeof part.text === "string"
176 |                   ? part.text
177 |                   : JSON.stringify(part.text, null, 2);
178 |               return (
179 |                 <div
180 |                   key={index}
181 |                   className="prose prose-invert max-w-none space-y-2 px-4 overflow-x-auto"
182 |                 >
183 |                   <MemoizedMarkdown id={message.id} content={textContent} />
184 |                 </div>
185 |               );
186 |             }
187 |             return null;
188 |           })
189 |         )}
190 |       </div>
191 |     </div>
192 |   );
193 | }

/components/tool-call-sequence.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | "use client";
 2 | 
 3 | import { useState } from "react";
 4 | import type { ToolInvocation } from "ai";
 5 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 6 | import {
 7 |   Collapsible,
 8 |   CollapsibleContent,
 9 |   CollapsibleTrigger,
10 | } from "@/components/ui/collapsible";
11 | import {
12 |   Loader2,
13 |   ChevronDown,
14 |   ChevronUp,
15 |   CheckCircle,
16 |   AlertCircle,
17 |   ListOrdered,
18 | } from "lucide-react";
19 | import { ToolCall } from "./tool-call";
20 | 
21 | interface ToolCallSequenceProps {
22 |   toolInvocations: ToolInvocation[];
23 | }
24 | 
25 | export function ToolCallSequence({ toolInvocations }: ToolCallSequenceProps) {
26 |   const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
27 | 
28 |   // Count completed and total tool calls
29 |   const completedCalls = toolInvocations.filter(
30 |     (t) => t.state === "result"
31 |   ).length;
32 |   const totalCalls = toolInvocations.length;
33 | 
34 |   // Check if all tool calls are complete
35 |   const allComplete = completedCalls === totalCalls;
36 |   // Check if any tool calls have errors
37 |   const hasErrors = false; // Placeholder: ToolInvocation.state from "ai" does not have an 'error' state.
38 |   // Check if any tool calls are still running (i.e., not in 'result' state yet)
39 |   const isLoading = toolInvocations.some(
40 |     (t) => t.state === "partial-call" || t.state === "call"
41 |   );
42 | 
43 |   return (
44 |     <div className="mt-3 border rounded-md overflow-hidden">
45 |       <Collapsible open={isOpen} onOpenChange={setIsOpen}>
46 |         <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-background border-b">
47 |           <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
48 |             {isLoading && (
49 |               <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
50 |             )}
51 |             {allComplete && !hasErrors && (
52 |               <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4 text-green-500" />
53 |             )}
54 |             {hasErrors && <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4 text-red-500" />}
55 |             <ListOrdered className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
56 |             <span className="font-medium">Tool Call Sequence</span>
57 |             <span className="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground/20">
58 |               {completedCalls}/{totalCalls} complete
59 |             </span>
60 |           </div>
61 | 
62 |           <CollapsibleTrigger asChild>
63 |             <Button variant="ghost" size="sm">
64 |               {isOpen ? (
65 |                 <ChevronUp className="h-4 w-4" />
66 |               ) : (
67 |                 <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4" />
68 |               )}
69 |             </Button>
70 |           </CollapsibleTrigger>
71 |         </div>
72 | 
73 |         <CollapsibleContent>
74 |           <div className="divide-y">
75 |             {toolInvocations.map((toolInvocation, index) => (
76 |               <div key={toolInvocation.toolCallId} className="p-2">
77 |                 <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
78 |                   <div className="flex items-center justify-center w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-muted text-xs font-medium">
79 |                     {index + 1}
80 |                   </div>
81 |                   <span className="text-sm font-medium">
82 |                     {toolInvocation.toolName}
83 |                   </span>
84 |                 </div>
85 |                 <ToolCall toolInvocation={toolInvocation} />
86 |               </div>
87 |             ))}
88 |           </div>
89 |         </CollapsibleContent>
90 |       </Collapsible>
91 |     </div>
92 |   );
93 | }

/components/tool-call.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | "use client";
 2 | 
 3 | import { useState } from "react";
 4 | import type { ToolInvocation } from "ai";
 5 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 6 | import {
 7 |   Collapsible,
 8 |   CollapsibleContent,
 9 |   CollapsibleTrigger,
10 | } from "@/components/ui/collapsible";
11 | import {
12 |   Loader2,
13 |   ChevronDown,
14 |   ChevronUp,
15 |   CheckCircle,
16 |   AlertCircle,
17 | } from "lucide-react";
18 | 
19 | interface ToolCallProps {
20 |   toolInvocation: ToolInvocation;
21 | }
22 | 
23 | export function ToolCall({ toolInvocation }: ToolCallProps) {
24 |   const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
25 |   const { toolName, state, args } = toolInvocation;
26 | 
27 |   const isLoading = state === "partial-call" || state === "call";
28 |   const isResultState = state === "result";
29 | 
30 |   const hasExplicitErrorState = false;
31 | 
32 |   let statusText = "Pending...";
33 |   if (isLoading) {
34 |     statusText = "Loading...";
35 |   } else if (isResultState) {
36 |     statusText = hasExplicitErrorState ? "Error" : "Complete";
37 |   }
38 | 
39 |   return (
40 |     <div className="mt-3 border rounded-md overflow-hidden">
41 |       <Collapsible open={isOpen} onOpenChange={setIsOpen}>
42 |         <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-background border-b">
43 |           <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
44 |             {isLoading && (
45 |               <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
46 |             )}
47 |             {isResultState && !hasExplicitErrorState && (
48 |               <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4 text-green-500" />
49 |             )}
50 |             {isResultState && hasExplicitErrorState && (
51 |               <AlertCircle className="h-4 w-4 text-red-500" />
52 |             )}
53 |             <span className="font-medium">{toolName}</span>
54 |             <span className="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground/20">
55 |               {statusText}
56 |             </span>
57 |           </div>
58 | 
59 |           <CollapsibleTrigger asChild>
60 |             <Button variant="ghost" size="sm">
61 |               {isOpen ? (
62 |                 <ChevronUp className="h-4 w-4" />
63 |               ) : (
64 |                 <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4" />
65 |               )}
66 |             </Button>
67 |           </CollapsibleTrigger>
68 |         </div>
69 | 
70 |         <CollapsibleContent>
71 |           <div className="p-3 bg-muted/50 border-b">
72 |             <h4 className="text-sm font-medium mb-1">Arguments</h4>
73 |             <pre className="text-xs bg-background p-2 rounded overflow-x-auto">
74 |               {JSON.stringify(args, null, 2)}
75 |             </pre>
76 |           </div>
77 | 
78 |           {isResultState && (
79 |             <div className="p-3 bg-background">
80 |               <h4 className="text-sm font-medium mb-1">
81 |                 {hasExplicitErrorState ? "Error Details" : "Result"}
82 |               </h4>
83 |               <pre className="text-xs bg-muted/50 p-2 rounded overflow-x-auto">
84 |                 {JSON.stringify(toolInvocation.result, null, 2)}
85 |               </pre>
86 |             </div>
87 |           )}
88 |         </CollapsibleContent>
89 |       </Collapsible>
90 |     </div>
91 |   );
92 | }
93 |

/components/tools-sidebar.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | /**
 2 |  * TODO: another vibe-coded component.
 3 |  * I think it's not working properly with nested fields,
 4 |  * i.e. z.number().describe("A number").optional() return description
 5 |  * but z.number().optional().describe("A number") does not.
 6 |  */
 7 | 
 8 | import { useEffect } from "react";
 9 | import mcpClient from "@/services/mcp/client";
10 | import { errorAtom, reloadToolsAtom } from "@/services/mcp/atoms";
11 | import { isMcpLoadingAtom } from "@/services/mcp/atoms";
12 | import { toolsAtom } from "@/services/mcp/atoms";
13 | import { useAtom, useAtomValue } from "jotai";
14 | import {
15 |   Accordion,
16 |   AccordionContent,
17 |   AccordionItem,
18 |   AccordionTrigger,
19 | } from "@/components/ui/accordion";
20 | 
21 | export function ToolsSidebar() {
22 |   const tools = useAtomValue(toolsAtom);
23 |   const isLoading = useAtomValue(isMcpLoadingAtom);
24 |   const error = useAtomValue(errorAtom);
25 |   const [reloadTools, setReloadTools] = useAtom(reloadToolsAtom);
26 | 
27 |   useEffect(() => {
28 |     if (reloadTools) {
29 |       mcpClient.getTools();
30 |       setReloadTools(false);
31 |     }
32 |   }, [reloadTools, setReloadTools]);
33 | 
34 |   return (
35 |     <div className="w-64 border-l flex flex-col h-full bg-sidebar-background dark:bg-sidebar-background">
36 |       <div className="p-4 border-b flex gap-2 items-center">
37 |         <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Available Tools</h2>
38 |         <a
39 |           className="text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground cursor-pointer"
40 |           onClick={async () => {
41 |             mcpClient.deleteTools();
42 |             await fetch("/api/tools", { method: "DELETE" });
43 |             setReloadTools(true);
44 |           }}
45 |         >
46 |           (Reset)
47 |         </a>
48 |       </div>
49 |       <div className="flex-grow overflow-y-auto">
50 |         <Accordion type="single" collapsible className="w-full">
51 |           {isLoading ? (
52 |             <div className="p-4 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
53 |               Loading tools...
54 |             </div>
55 |           ) : error ? (
56 |             <div className="p-4 text-sm text-red-500">{error}</div>
57 |           ) : (
58 |             tools &&
59 |             tools.breakdown &&
60 |             Object.entries(tools.breakdown).map(([server, tools]) => (
61 |               <AccordionItem key={server} value={server}>
62 |                 <div className="p-4 border-b last:border-b-0 hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-700">
63 |                   <AccordionTrigger>{server}</AccordionTrigger>
64 |                   <AccordionContent>
65 |                     <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
66 |                       {Object.entries(tools).map(([name, tool]) => (
67 |                         <div key={`${server}-${name}`}>
68 |                           <p className="text-sm font-medium">{name}</p>
69 |                           <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
70 |                             {tool.description}
71 |                           </p>
72 |                         </div>
73 |                       ))}
74 |                     </div>
75 |                   </AccordionContent>
76 |                 </div>
77 |               </AccordionItem>
78 |             ))
79 |           )}
80 |         </Accordion>
81 |       </div>
82 |     </div>
83 |   );
84 | }
85 |

/components/ui/sidebar.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | "use client";
  2 | 
  3 | import * as React from "react";
  4 | import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
  5 | import { VariantProps, cva } from "class-variance-authority";
  6 | import { PanelLeftIcon } from "lucide-react";
  7 | 
  8 | import { useIsMobile } from "@/hooks/use-mobile";
  9 | import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 10 | import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 11 | import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
 12 | import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
 13 | import {
 14 |   Sheet,
 15 |   SheetContent,
 16 |   SheetDescription,
 17 |   SheetHeader,
 18 |   SheetTitle,
 19 | } from "@/components/ui/sheet";
 20 | import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
 21 | import {
 22 |   Tooltip,
 23 |   TooltipContent,
 24 |   TooltipProvider,
 25 |   TooltipTrigger,
 26 | } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 27 | 
 28 | const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME = "sidebar_state";
 29 | const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE = 60 * 60 * 24 * 7;
 30 | const SIDEBAR_WIDTH = "20rem";
 31 | const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE = "18rem";
 32 | const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON = "3rem";
 33 | const SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT = "b";
 34 | 
 35 | type SidebarContextProps = {
 36 |   state: "expanded" | "collapsed";
 37 |   open: boolean;
 38 |   setOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
 39 |   openMobile: boolean;
 40 |   setOpenMobile: (open: boolean) => void;
 41 |   isMobile: boolean;
 42 |   toggleSidebar: () => void;
 43 | };
 44 | 
 45 | const SidebarContext = React.createContext<SidebarContextProps | null>(null);
 46 | 
 47 | function useSidebar() {
 48 |   const context = React.useContext(SidebarContext);
 49 |   if (!context) {
 50 |     throw new Error("useSidebar must be used within a SidebarProvider.");
 51 |   }
 52 | 
 53 |   return context;
 54 | }
 55 | 
 56 | function SidebarProvider({
 57 |   defaultOpen = true,
 58 |   open: openProp,
 59 |   onOpenChange: setOpenProp,
 60 |   className,
 61 |   style,
 62 |   children,
 63 |   ...props
 64 | }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
 65 |   defaultOpen?: boolean;
 66 |   open?: boolean;
 67 |   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
 68 | }) {
 69 |   const isMobile = useIsMobile();
 70 |   const [openMobile, setOpenMobile] = React.useState(false);
 71 | 
 72 |   // This is the internal state of the sidebar.
 73 |   // We use openProp and setOpenProp for control from outside the component.
 74 |   const [_open, _setOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen);
 75 |   const open = openProp ?? _open;
 76 |   const setOpen = React.useCallback(
 77 |     (value: boolean | ((value: boolean) => boolean)) => {
 78 |       const openState = typeof value === "function" ? value(open) : value;
 79 |       if (setOpenProp) {
 80 |         setOpenProp(openState);
 81 |       } else {
 82 |         _setOpen(openState);
 83 |       }
 84 | 
 85 |       // This sets the cookie to keep the sidebar state.
 86 |       document.cookie = `${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME}=${openState}; path=/; max-age=${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE}`;
 87 |     },
 88 |     [setOpenProp, open]
 89 |   );
 90 | 
 91 |   // Helper to toggle the sidebar.
 92 |   const toggleSidebar = React.useCallback(() => {
 93 |     return isMobile ? setOpenMobile((open) => !open) : setOpen((open) => !open);
 94 |   }, [isMobile, setOpen, setOpenMobile]);
 95 | 
 96 |   // Adds a keyboard shortcut to toggle the sidebar.
 97 |   React.useEffect(() => {
 98 |     const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
 99 |       if (
100 |         event.key === SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT &&
101 |         (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)
102 |       ) {
103 |         event.preventDefault();
104 |         toggleSidebar();
105 |       }
106 |     };
107 | 
108 |     window.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
109 |     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
110 |   }, [toggleSidebar]);
111 | 
112 |   // We add a state so that we can do data-state="expanded" or "collapsed".
113 |   // This makes it easier to style the sidebar with Tailwind classes.
114 |   const state = open ? "expanded" : "collapsed";
115 | 
116 |   const contextValue = React.useMemo<SidebarContextProps>(
117 |     () => ({
118 |       state,
119 |       open,
120 |       setOpen,
121 |       isMobile,
122 |       openMobile,
123 |       setOpenMobile,
124 |       toggleSidebar,
125 |     }),
126 |     [state, open, setOpen, isMobile, openMobile, setOpenMobile, toggleSidebar]
127 |   );
128 | 
129 |   return (
130 |     <SidebarContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
131 |       <TooltipProvider delayDuration={0}>
132 |         <div
133 |           data-slot="sidebar-wrapper"
134 |           style={
135 |             {
136 |               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH,
137 |               "--sidebar-width-icon": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON,
138 |               ...style,
139 |             } as React.CSSProperties
140 |           }
141 |           className={cn(
142 |             "group/sidebar-wrapper has-data-[variant=inset]:bg-sidebar flex min-h-svh w-full",
143 |             className
144 |           )}
145 |           {...props}
146 |         >
147 |           {children}
148 |         </div>
149 |       </TooltipProvider>
150 |     </SidebarContext.Provider>
151 |   );
152 | }
153 | 
154 | function Sidebar({
155 |   side = "left",
156 |   variant = "sidebar",
157 |   collapsible = "offcanvas",
158 |   className,
159 |   children,
160 |   ...props
161 | }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
162 |   side?: "left" | "right";
163 |   variant?: "sidebar" | "floating" | "inset";
164 |   collapsible?: "offcanvas" | "icon" | "none";
165 | }) {
166 |   const { isMobile, state, openMobile, setOpenMobile } = useSidebar();
167 | 
168 |   if (collapsible === "none") {
169 |     return (
170 |       <div
171 |         data-slot="sidebar"
172 |         className={cn(
173 |           "bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground flex h-full w-(--sidebar-width) flex-col",
174 |           className
175 |         )}
176 |         {...props}
177 |       >
178 |         {children}
179 |       </div>
180 |     );
181 |   }
182 | 
183 |   if (isMobile) {
184 |     return (
185 |       <Sheet open={openMobile} onOpenChange={setOpenMobile} {...props}>
186 |         <SheetContent
187 |           data-sidebar="sidebar"
188 |           data-slot="sidebar"
189 |           data-mobile="true"
190 |           className="bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground w-(--sidebar-width) p-0 [&>button]:hidden"
191 |           style={
192 |             {
193 |               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE,
194 |             } as React.CSSProperties
195 |           }
196 |           side={side}
197 |         >
198 |           <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
199 |             <SheetTitle>Sidebar</SheetTitle>
200 |             <SheetDescription>Displays the mobile sidebar.</SheetDescription>
201 |           </SheetHeader>
202 |           <div className="flex h-full w-full flex-col">{children}</div>
203 |         </SheetContent>
204 |       </Sheet>
205 |     );
206 |   }
207 | 
208 |   return (
209 |     <div
210 |       className="group peer text-sidebar-foreground hidden md:block"
211 |       data-state={state}
212 |       data-collapsible={state === "collapsed" ? collapsible : ""}
213 |       data-variant={variant}
214 |       data-side={side}
215 |       data-slot="sidebar"
216 |     >
217 |       {/* This is what handles the sidebar gap on desktop */}
218 |       <div
219 |         data-slot="sidebar-gap"
220 |         className={cn(
221 |           "relative w-(--sidebar-width) bg-transparent transition-[width] duration-200 ease-linear",
222 |           "group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:w-0",
223 |           "group-data-[side=right]:rotate-180",
224 |           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
225 |             ? "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4)))]"
226 |             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon)"
227 |         )}
228 |       />
229 |       <div
230 |         data-slot="sidebar-container"
231 |         className={cn(
232 |           "fixed inset-y-0 z-10 hidden h-svh w-(--sidebar-width) transition-[left,right,width] duration-200 ease-linear md:flex",
233 |           side === "left"
234 |             ? "left-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:left-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]"
235 |             : "right-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:right-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]",
236 |           // Adjust the padding for floating and inset variants.
237 |           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
238 |             ? "p-2 group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4))+2px)]"
239 |             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon) group-data-[side=left]:border-r group-data-[side=right]:border-l",
240 |           className
241 |         )}
242 |         {...props}
243 |       >
244 |         <div
245 |           data-sidebar="sidebar"
246 |           data-slot="sidebar-inner"
247 |           className="bg-sidebar group-data-[variant=floating]:border-sidebar-border flex h-full w-full flex-col group-data-[variant=floating]:rounded-lg group-data-[variant=floating]:border group-data-[variant=floating]:shadow-sm"
248 |         >
249 |           {children}
250 |         </div>
251 |       </div>
252 |     </div>
253 |   );
254 | }
255 |

498 | function SidebarMenuButton({
499 |   asChild = false,
500 |   isActive = false,
501 |   variant = "default",
502 |   size = "default",
503 |   tooltip,
504 |   className,
505 |   ...props
506 | }: React.ComponentProps<"button"> & {
507 |   asChild?: boolean;
508 |   isActive?: boolean;
509 |   tooltip?: string | React.ComponentProps<typeof TooltipContent>;
510 | } & VariantProps<typeof sidebarMenuButtonVariants>) {
511 |   const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button";
512 |   const { isMobile, state } = useSidebar();
513 | 
514 |   const button = (
515 |     <Comp
516 |       data-slot="sidebar-menu-button"
517 |       data-sidebar="menu-button"
518 |       data-size={size}
519 |       data-active={isActive}
520 |       className={cn(sidebarMenuButtonVariants({ variant, size }), className)}
521 |       {...props}
522 |     />
523 |   );
524 | 
525 |   if (!tooltip) {
526 |     return button;
527 |   }
528 | 
529 |   if (typeof tooltip === "string") {
530 |     tooltip = {
531 |       children: tooltip,
532 |     };
533 |   }
534 | 
535 |   return (
536 |     <Tooltip>
537 |       <TooltipTrigger asChild>{button}</TooltipTrigger>
538 |       <TooltipContent
539 |         side="right"
540 |         align="center"
541 |         hidden={state !== "collapsed" || isMobile}
542 |         {...tooltip}
543 |       />
544 |     </Tooltip>
545 |   );
546 | }

/hooks/use-mobile.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import * as React from "react"
 2 | 
 3 | const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768
 4 | 
 5 | export function useIsMobile() {
 6 |   const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined)
 7 | 
 8 |   React.useEffect(() => {
 9 |     const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`)
10 |     const onChange = () => {
11 |       setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
12 |     }
13 |     mql.addEventListener("change", onChange)
14 |     setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
15 |     return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange)
16 |   }, [])
17 | 
18 |   return !!isMobile
19 | }
20 | 


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/lib/tools.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | import { Tool, tool } from "ai";
  2 | import { experimental_createMCPClient as createMCPClient } from "ai";
  3 | import {
  4 |   StdioConfig,
  5 |   Experimental_StdioMCPTransport as StdioMCPTransport,
  6 | } from "ai/mcp-stdio";
  7 | import { readFile } from "fs/promises";
  8 | import { join } from "path";
  9 | 
 10 | import { z } from "zod";
 11 | 
 12 | const tools: Record<string, Tool> = {
 13 |   dummyTool: tool({
 14 |     description: "Dummy tool for demo purposes and testing.",
 15 |     parameters: z.object({
 16 |       location: z
 17 |         .string()
 18 |         .describe("The city and state, e.g. San Francisco, CA"),
 19 |     }),
 20 |     execute: async ({ location }) => {
 21 |       // Mock weather data
 22 |       const conditions = ["Sunny", "Cloudy", "Rainy", "Snowy", "Partly Cloudy"];
 23 |       const temperature = Math.floor(Math.random() * 35) + 40; // 40-75°F
 24 |       const humidity = Math.floor(Math.random() * 50) + 30; // 30-80%
 25 | 
 26 |       return {
 27 |         location,
 28 |         temperature,
 29 |         condition: conditions[Math.floor(Math.random() * conditions.length)],
 30 |         humidity,
 31 |         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
 32 |       };
 33 |     },
 34 |   }),
 35 | };
 36 | 
 37 | export const getTools = async () => {
 38 |   try {
 39 |     /**
 40 |      * Not ideal, but we're basically starting/stopping STDIO processes
 41 |      * for every tool call.
 42 |      */
 43 |     // Read mcptools.json if it exists, otherwise initialize an empty object
 44 |     const MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH = join(process.cwd(), "mcptools.json");
 45 | 
 46 |     let mcpToolsJson: { mcpServers: Record<string, StdioConfig> } = {
 47 |       mcpServers: {},
 48 |     };
 49 |     try {
 50 |       const fileContent = await readFile(MCP_TOOLS_FILEPATH, "utf8");
 51 |       mcpToolsJson = JSON.parse(fileContent);
 52 |     } catch {
 53 |       // File does not exist or is invalid, initialize as empty object
 54 |       mcpToolsJson = { mcpServers: {} };
 55 |     }
 56 | 
 57 |     // Flatten all MCP tools into one big object
 58 |     const mcpTools: Record<string, Tool> = {};
 59 |     const mcpBreakdown: Record<string, Record<string, Tool>> = {};
 60 | 
 61 |     if (!mcpToolsJson.mcpServers) {
 62 |       mcpToolsJson.mcpServers = {};
 63 |     }
 64 |     const closeClients = await Promise.all(
 65 |       Object.entries(mcpToolsJson.mcpServers).map(
 66 |         async ([serverName, server]) => {
 67 |           console.log("SERVER", server);
 68 |           const mcpClient = await createMCPClient({
 69 |             transport: new StdioMCPTransport(server),
 70 |           });
 71 | 
 72 |           const toolsFromServer = await mcpClient.tools();
 73 |           Object.assign(mcpTools, toolsFromServer);
 74 |           mcpBreakdown[serverName] = toolsFromServer;
 75 |           // Return an async function that closes this client
 76 |           return async () => {
 77 |             await mcpClient.close();
 78 |           };
 79 |         }
 80 |       )
 81 |     );
 82 | 
 83 |     return {
 84 |       tools: {
 85 |         ...mcpTools,
 86 |         ...tools,
 87 |       },
 88 |       breakdown: mcpBreakdown,
 89 |       closeClients: async () => {
 90 |         await Promise.all(closeClients.map((closeClient) => closeClient()));
 91 |       },
 92 |     };
 93 |   } catch (error) {
 94 |     console.error("Error initializing MCP client:", error);
 95 |     // Fallback to just the local tools if MCP client fails
 96 |     return {
 97 |       tools,
 98 |       closeClients: async () => {},
 99 |     };
100 |   }
101 | };
102 |

 10 |   parentId: undefined,
 11 |   detached: false,
 12 |   date: new Date().toISOString(),
 13 |   metadata: {
 14 |     message: {
 15 |       role: "system",
 16 |       content: "Initial commit",
 17 |       id: "ROOT_COMMIT",
 18 |     },
 19 |   },
 20 | };
 21 | 
 22 | export const commitsAtom = atomWithStorage<Record<string, Commit>>("commits", {
 23 |   [ROOT_COMMIT.id]: ROOT_COMMIT,
 24 | });
 25 | export const commitHeadAtom = atomWithStorage<string>(
 26 |   "commitHead",
 27 |   ROOT_COMMIT.id
 28 | );
 29 | export const loadingCommitThreadAtom = atom(false);
 30 | export const AISDKMessagesAtom = atom<Message[]>([]);
 31 | export const isLoadingAtom = atom(false);
 32 | 
 33 | /**
 34 |  * Get the active commit thread as a list of commits.
 35 |  * @returns The commit thread, or undefined if not found.
 36 |  */
 37 | export const commitThreadAtom = atom((get) => {
 38 |   const commits = get(commitsAtom);
 39 |   const commitHead = get(commitHeadAtom);
 40 |   // Create a map for quick lookup by id
 41 |   const commitMap = new Map(Object.values(commits).map((c) => [c.id, c]));
 42 |   let node = commitHead ? commits[commitHead] : null;
 43 |   const result: Commit[] = [];
 44 |   let i = 0;
 45 |   while (node && i < Object.keys(commits).length) {
 46 |     result.push(node);
 47 |     if (!node.parentId || node.detached) break;
 48 |     node = commitMap.get(node.parentId) ?? null;
 49 |     i++;
 50 |   }
 51 |   result.reverse();
 52 | 
 53 |   //   console.log("TEST COMMIT CALLED HERE", commits, commitHead, result);
 54 |   return result;
 55 | });
 56 | 
 57 | /**
 58 |  * Get the full list of commits, including detached commits for the sidebar.
 59 |  * @returns The full list of commits.
 60 |  */
 61 | export const fullCommitListAtom = atom((get) => {
 62 |   const commits = get(commitsAtom);
 63 |   return Object.values(commits);
 64 | });
 65 | 
 66 | /**
 67 |  * Get the indices of the children of the current commit within fullCommitListAtom.
 68 |  * i.e. { commit.id : index }
 69 |  * @returns The indices of the children of the current commit within fullCommitListAtom.
 70 |  */
 71 | export const currentCommitChildrenAtom = atom((get) => {
 72 |   console.log("CURRENT COMMIT CHILDREN CALLED");
 73 |   const commitList = get(fullCommitListAtom);
 74 |   const commitHead = get(commitHeadAtom);
 75 |   const children = commitList.filter((c) => {
 76 |     return c.parentId === commitHead && !c.detached;
 77 |   });
 78 |   return children;
 79 | });
 80 | 
 81 | export const currentCommitChildrenIndexMapAtom = atom((get) => {
 82 |   const children = get(currentCommitChildrenAtom);
 83 |   // Collapse children into a map of { commit.id : index }
 84 |   const childrenMap: Record<string, number> = {};
 85 |   children.forEach((c, idx) => {
 86 |     childrenMap[c.id] = idx;
 87 |   });
 88 |   console.log("THREAD CHILDREN", childrenMap);
 89 |   return childrenMap;
 90 | });
 91 | 
 92 | /**
 93 |  * Get the last commit from the user.
 94 |  * @returns The last commit from the user, or undefined if not found.
 95 |  */
 96 | export const lastUserCommitAtom = atom((get) => {
 97 |   const commits = get(commitsAtom);
 98 |   const commitHead = get(commitHeadAtom);
 99 |   let currentId: string | null = commitHead;
100 |   let node = undefined;
101 |   while (currentId) {
102 |     const commit: Commit | undefined = commits[currentId];
103 |     if (!commit) break;
104 |     if (commit.author === "user") {
105 |       node = commit;
106 |       break;
107 |     }
108 |     currentId = commit.parentId ?? null;
109 |   }
110 |   return node;
111 | });
112 |

/services/gitchat/client.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | import { Message } from "ai";
  2 | import { Commit as ICommit } from ".";
  3 | import {
  4 |   commitHeadAtom,
  5 |   commitsAtom,
  6 |   commitThreadAtom,
  7 |   lastUserCommitAtom,
  8 |   ROOT_COMMIT,
  9 | } from "./atoms";
 10 | import { getDefaultStore } from "jotai";
 11 | import { GitChatClient } from ".";
 12 | 
 13 | export type Commit = ICommit & {
 14 |   metadata: {
 15 |     message: Message;
 16 |   };
 17 | };
 18 | 
 19 | export class GitChat implements GitChatClient {
 20 |   private get state() {
 21 |     const store = getDefaultStore();
 22 |     return store;
 23 |   }
 24 | 
 25 |   public get commits() {
 26 |     return this.state.get(commitsAtom);
 27 |   }
 28 | 
 29 |   public get commitHead() {
 30 |     return this.state.get(commitHeadAtom);
 31 |   }
 32 | 
 33 |   public get commitThread() {
 34 |     return this.state.get(commitThreadAtom);
 35 |   }
 36 | 
 37 |   private set commits(commits: Record<string, Commit>) {
 38 |     this.state.set(commitsAtom, commits);
 39 |   }
 40 | 
 41 |   /**
 42 |    * Initialize the GitChat client.
 43 |    */
 44 |   public static init(): GitChat {
 45 |     return new GitChat();
 46 |   }
 47 | 
 48 |   /**
 49 |    * Add a commit to the chat.
 50 |    * @param commit - The commit to add.
 51 |    */
 52 |   public addCommit(commit: Commit, replace?: boolean): void {
 53 |     if (replace && !this.commits[commit.id]) {
 54 |       this.commits = { ...this.commits, [commit.id]: commit };
 55 |     }
 56 |   }
 57 | 
 58 |   /**
 59 |    * Clear the commits from the chat tree.
 60 |    */
 61 |   public clearCommits(hardDelete?: boolean): void {
 62 |     if (hardDelete) {
 63 |       this.commits = {};
 64 |     }
 65 |     this.state.set(commitHeadAtom, ROOT_COMMIT.id);
 66 |   }
 67 | 
 68 |   /**
 69 |    * Detach a commit from the chat.
 70 |    * @param commitId - The id of the commit to detach.
 71 |    */
 72 |   public detachCommit(commitId: string): void {
 73 |     this.commits[commitId].detached = true;
 74 |     this.commits = { ...this.commits };
 75 |   }
 76 | 
 77 |   /**
 78 |    * Retach a commit back to its head
 79 |    * @param commitId - The id of the commit to retach.
 80 |    */
 81 |   public retachCommit(commitId: string): void {
 82 |     this.commits[commitId].detached = false;
 83 |     this.commits = { ...this.commits };
 84 |   }
 85 | 
 86 |   public setCommitHead(commitId: string): void {
 87 |     this.state.set(commitHeadAtom, commitId);
 88 |   }
 89 | 
 90 |   /**
 91 |    * Allows the user to effectively start a new chat branch from the last user commit.
 92 |    */
 93 |   public redoLastUserCommit(): string | undefined {
 94 |     const lastUserCommit = this.state.get(lastUserCommitAtom);
 95 |     if (!lastUserCommit || !lastUserCommit.parentId) return;
 96 |     this.setCommitHead(lastUserCommit.parentId);
 97 |   }
 98 | }
 99 | 
100 | const gitChat = GitChat.init();
101 | export default gitChat;
102 |

/services/gitchat/index.d.ts:

 1 | /**
 2 |  * Represents a commit in the GitChat system.
 3 |  * @property {string} id - The unique identifier for the commit.
 4 |  * @property {string} message - The commit message describing the change.
 5 |  * @property {string} author - The author of the commit.
 6 |  * @property {string} date - The ISO string date of the commit.
 7 |  * @property {string} [parentId] - The ID of the parent commit, if any.
 8 |  * @property {object} [metadata] - Optional additional metadata for the commit.
 9 |  */
10 | export interface Commit {
11 |   id: string;
12 |   message: string;
13 |   author: string;
14 |   date: string;
15 |   parentId?: string;
16 |   detached?: boolean;
17 |   metadata?: object;
18 | }
19 | 
20 | export interface GitChatClient {
21 |   /**
22 |    * Add a commit to the chat.
23 |    * @param commit - The commit to add (partial to allow for auto-generated fields like id and date).
24 |    * @returns The chat object.
25 |    */
26 |   addCommit(commit: Partial<Commit>): void;
27 |   clearCommits(): void;
28 |   detachCommit(commitId: string): void;
29 |   retachCommit(commitId: string): void;
30 | }
31 |

 6 |   null
 7 | );
 8 | export const isMcpLoadingAtom = atom<boolean>(true);
 9 | export const errorAtom = atom<string | null>(null);
10 | export const reloadToolsAtom = atom<boolean>(true);
11 | export const breakdownAtom = atom<Record<string, Record<string, Tool>> | null>(
12 |   null
13 | );
14 | export const isMcpConfigOpenAtom = atom<boolean>(false);

/services/mcp/client.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1 | import { Tool } from "ai";
  2 | import { getDefaultStore } from "jotai";
  3 | import {
  4 |   toolsAtom,
  5 |   isMcpLoadingAtom,
  6 |   errorAtom,
  7 |   breakdownAtom,
  8 |   isMcpConfigOpenAtom,
  9 |   serverConfigAtom,
 10 | } from "./atoms";
 11 | 
 12 | class MCPClient {
 13 |   private get state() {
 14 |     const store = getDefaultStore();
 15 |     return store;
 16 |   }
 17 |   private setTools(tools: Record<string, Record<string, Tool>>) {
 18 |     this.state.set(toolsAtom, tools);
 19 |   }
 20 |   private setIsLoading(isLoading: boolean) {
 21 |     this.state.set(isMcpLoadingAtom, isLoading);
 22 |   }
 23 |   private setError(error: string) {
 24 |     this.state.set(errorAtom, error);
 25 |   }
 26 |   private setBreakdown(breakdown: Record<string, Record<string, Tool>>) {
 27 |     this.state.set(breakdownAtom, breakdown);
 28 |   }
 29 |   private setIsOpen(isOpen: boolean) {
 30 |     this.state.set(isMcpConfigOpenAtom, isOpen);
 31 |   }
 32 |   private setServerConfig(serverConfig: Record<string, unknown>) {
 33 |     this.state.set(serverConfigAtom, serverConfig);
 34 |   }
 35 | 
 36 |   private get serverConfig() {
 37 |     return this.state.get(serverConfigAtom);
 38 |   }
 39 | 
 40 |   public parseServerConfig(mcpServersText: string) {
 41 |     try {
 42 |       const parsed = JSON.parse(mcpServersText);
 43 |       this.setServerConfig(parsed);
 44 |     } catch {
 45 |       this.setError("Invalid JSON");
 46 |     }
 47 |   }
 48 | 
 49 |   public async getTools(): Promise<void> {
 50 |     try {
 51 |       const response = await fetch("/api/tools");
 52 |       if (!response.ok) {
 53 |         throw new Error("Failed to fetch tools");
 54 |       }
 55 |       const data = await response.json();
 56 |       this.setTools({ breakdown: data.breakdown });
 57 |       this.setBreakdown(data.breakdown);
 58 |       this.setServerConfig(data.config || { mcpServers: {} });
 59 |     } catch (err) {
 60 |       this.setError(
 61 |         err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to load tools"
 62 |       );
 63 |     } finally {
 64 |       this.setIsLoading(false);
 65 |     }
 66 |   }
 67 | 
 68 |   public async deleteTools(): Promise<void> {
 69 |     this.setTools({});
 70 |   }
 71 | 
 72 |   public async handleSave() {
 73 |     try {
 74 |       this.setIsLoading(true);
 75 |       await this.saveServerConfig();
 76 |       this.setIsOpen(false);
 77 |       await this.getTools();
 78 |     } catch (error) {
 79 |       console.error("Error saving server config:", error);
 80 |     } finally {
 81 |       this.setIsLoading(false);
 82 |     }
 83 |   }
 84 |   public async saveServerConfig() {
 85 |     try {
 86 |       const response = await fetch("/api/tools", {
 87 |         method: "POST",
 88 |         headers: {
 89 |           "Content-Type": "application/json",
 90 |         },
 91 |         body: JSON.stringify(this.serverConfig),
 92 |       });
 93 |       const data = await response.json();
 94 |       console.log("Tools saved:", data);
 95 |     } catch (error) {
 96 |       console.error("Error saving tools:", error);
 97 |       throw error;
 98 |     }
 99 |   }
100 | }
101 | 
102 | const mcpClient = new MCPClient();
103 | export default mcpClient;
104 |
